Post-War Inspection of the Jinpu Line (Continued) 68

The Calamity of the Taian Military Disaster. The reporters arrived in Taian at 4 pm on the 1st and immediately went to the headquarters of the 15th Route Army to visit. It happened that Commander-in-Chief Ma Hongkui had gone to Jinan to report and had not returned, so he was received by Chief of Staff Luo Zhen. According to Luo, the Central Army captured Taian Station on the 5th. The enemy entered the city on the 6th to resist. Cai Yan'kai's division besieged the city on the 8th.

The army took over the siege on the 9th and twice threw letters to Huang Shitong, the brigade commander of the 12th Brigade of the Jin Army defending the city, urging him to surrender. Huang initially did not answer, but the second time Huang replied in a letter, roughly saying that he could not have both integrity and life, and he would rather sacrifice his life to defend the city. Therefore, the army had no choice but to bomb the city, etc. On the morning of the 2nd, the reporters entered the city and visited the headquarters of the 64th Division to visit Division Commander Ma Tengjiao. According to Ma, the division captured Ningyang on the 4th, passed Wenkou on the 6th, and arrived here on the 8th to take over the siege. When Commander-in-Chief Liu lived in Honggou, he ordered the city to be attacked. Tai City was built of stone and could not be opened urgently. Commander-in-Chief Liu personally went to Tai Station and climbed Haoli Mountain to command, but it was also ineffective. I inspected the city around the foot of Mount Tai on the 11th

So I decided to dig a tunnel. At the southwest gate, I started digging during the daytime gunfire. On the 22nd, 400 pounds of explosives were transported. Because the amount was small, it was completely installed in the tunnel at the west gate. On the 23rd, another 400 pounds were transported from Jinan and also installed in the tunnel at the west gate. On the 24th, the bricks and stones were bombed two or three hundred meters at dawn. The residents outside the city had been secretly ordered to move the day before, so no people died. The division took the opportunity to attack and fought in the alleys for two hours before disarming the remnants of the enemy in the north of the city, the Dai Temple, and the southeast and southwest gates. My brigade commander

Ma Quanliang was injured in the leg when he captured Huang Tuling and is still receiving medical treatment in Jinan. Then I went to inspect the city. Outside the west gate, the outer city was bombed to the root, and rubble was piled up. The tunnel was about seven feet deep and four feet long. It was completed from the 19th to the 23rd. From the city

Outside the Taiji Stone Printing Bureau, it leads to the Chinese and Western pharmacies inside the city. Among the destroyed houses, there are seven or eight houses including the mainland bookstore and the Chengwen Bookstore, twelve rooms of the Daosheng Tea Shop, five Chinese and Western pharmacies,

Five Taiji Stone Printing Bureaus, five Taihe Foreign Goods Stores, and

Six Zheng's Ironware Stores, a total of more than 60 rooms, all became powder. The Dai Temple in the northeast corner of the city was also hit by many shells. The west mountain corner of the Junji Hall has been bombed down. When the Jin army defended the city, the people were afraid of planes and bombs and mostly hid outside the Dai Temple. The Shanmen is a door that is slightly like a city wall. The people dug holes in the door wall to live in, and then they were driven away by the Jin army and moved to the cave, so there were many surrenders in the Dai Temple when the city was broken. Huang Shitong, the brigade commander of the Jin army, initially fed the residents, and then moved to the Tiantai Yinhang. All circles once asked Huang not to hold on to the city store to the death, but Huang falsely refused. When Brigade Commander Ma Quanliang entered the city, he did not know where Huang was, so he tore off his armband and pretended to be a Jin army, shouting that the enemy had entered the city and that the brothers should protect the brigade commander. Someone responded and said that the brigade commander was in the Dai Temple, so go protect him quickly. Ma ran to the Dai Temple and shouted, "Where is the brigade commander? Let's protect him!"

Huang's guards replied, "The brigade commander is here." Ma immediately jumped forward and captured Huang, but was injured in the leg by Huang's guards. The city was fought in separate alleys, so the civilian houses were either broken into

Holes or completely collapsed, and there was no time to see them. According to the latest survey by the Public Security Bureau, 44 people died and 68 were injured in the city, and 1,513 houses were damaged, worth about 63,230 yuan. The losses outside the city are still being investigated. It is indeed a great catastrophe that Taicheng has never had before. At 12:00 noon, I climbed Mount Tai and inspected along the way, passing through Yitiandoumugong Hutian Pavilion Yueling to Zhongtianmen. There is a

Cai Tingkai's division dug a trench that extends east to Zhongqi Mountain in the west to Baiyangfangding, which is very long. Going up to Nantianmen again,

It is especially dangerous. There is a battle trench of the Jin army in the center of Nantianmen, with machine gun positions set up on both sides, extending along the peaks. The houses in Zhongtianmen and Nantianmen were damaged. According to the scholars on the mountain, Liu Zhaotang, the brigade commander of the 21st Brigade of the 15th Army of the Jin Army, retreated from the foot of the mountain on the 15th. Cai Tingcuo returned and pursued from behind. Liu Brigade defended Nantianmen, waiting for reinforcements. Coupled with the continuous heavy rain, he could not retreat from behind the mountain, so he had to try his best to defend. The vanguard of Cai's division attacked the Shouxing Pavilion under Nantianmen, but the rear team did not arrive, so they retreated to Zhongtianmen and blocked the road. The next day, Cai's division exchanged defenses with Ma's division. At this time, the Jin army attacked from Laolongzhai, took Zhongqi Mountain, and took Baiyangding from Lanzhu Mountain, and forced down from the stone steps of Nantianmen in the middle. Ma's division retreated to Yemaling and immediately counterattacked.

The attack continued to Zhongtianmen, and the fierce battles on the 18th and 19th were the most intense. There were three trips between Zhongnan and Nantianmen in one day. Afterwards, Ma's division went around Heilongtan from Diumugong and copied to Yuhuangding to intercept the rear of the Jin army at Nantianmen. The Jin army could not support it and retreated in chaos from behind the mountain. Several Jin army corpses were buried under Daibusong above Hongqiaofeipu (the mountain chair is the sedan chair that goes up the mountain). The people who passed there still pointed and told each other. However, before the Jin army retreated, Liu Zhaotang abandoned his

The ministry secretly ordered the Taoist priests to lead the way from the back mountain, so he was spared being captured. That night, the reporters stayed at Yuhuangding. They went down the mountain at 2:00 pm on the third morning and boarded the train north again. According to this observation, Taian suffered a great disaster. The number of manual carts heard about requisitioned was as many as 3,000.

A Glimpse of the Current Situation in Jining Port. The reporter group left Tai at noon on the 3rd and headed north. South of Jieshou, they saw another trench of the Jin army. North of Taian, a bridge was destroyed. There was an anti-aircraft gun position at Wandezhan. After passing this, they did not see any traces of war. After the Jin army was defeated in Taian, they retreated to the north bank of the river. When they first retreated to the north bank, they only left a few troops in the north of Luokou. Recently, they have increased their troops again. Since the 1st, they have been fighting with the Central Army across the river. The Central Army's Li Yunheng Division is guarding west of Luokou, and the First Army Group is guarding east of Luokou. The defense is very solid. The Jin army is not formally counterattacking, but is actually coordinating with the Feng army on the Longhai Line, etc. Then I visited Acting Chairman Yuan Jiapu at the Provincial Government. According to the conversation,

The difficulties of the provincial government are extremely extreme. After the military affairs, the magistrates of the counties are all appointed by the various armies for convenience. The tax money is intercepted by each and sent to the headquarters, so the provincial government can hardly take measures for the county administration of the outer counties. Jinan was not disturbed when the Jin army retreated, etc. Although the local order in Jinan can be heard from Luokou at that time, the artillery fire is still quiet. The reporter group rested for a day on the 6th and decided to return to Xuzhou on a one-time train on the evening of the 7th (6th).

Guangdong Merchants Request Improvement of Stamp Duty Regulations 69

The General Chamber of Commerce Will Organize a Discussion Meeting. The City Chamber of Commerce Proposes Improvement Proposals. Guangzhou Correspondence: The Provisional Regulations on Stamp Duty Law in Guangdong were promulgated on January 1, 1926. At that time, it was only an expedient measure to raise money, so there was the word "provisional." Since then, it has been used as an example and implemented to this day without being revoked. Moreover, the stamp duty law differs from the stamp duty law promulgated by the central government.

It is very necessary to abolish the provisional regulations promulgated in Guangdong. Not only has it not been abolished, but in recent years, abuses have grown. The Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce convened a special meeting of merchants on the 6th to

Discuss the issue of the survival of this provisional ordinance. More than forty representatives of various industries attended the meeting that day. At 1:30 pm, the

Meeting was held, and Huang Yong was elected as the interim chairman to announce the origin of the provisional stamp

Regulations and the abuses that have occurred in recent days. Please have each representative express as many opinions as possible so that a memorial can be drafted and submitted to the Finance Bureau for review. Chen read out proposals from the Silver Industry, the Rice and Sugar Association, and the Rice Merchants Association, emphasizing that the provisional regulations have been

For years, it has been harsh on the business community, and special requests have been made for improvement or revocation to alleviate the suffering of the merchants. Synthesizing all opinions, Group A advocated submitting a request to the Finance Bureau to amend the regulations. Group

Page 12

Group B advocated submitting a request to revoke the regulations fundamentally. As a result of the vote, the Guangdong Stamp Duty Provisional Regulations Discussion Committee was organized, and Peng Chuli and other fifteen business directors were immediately elected as drafting

The members and requested the government to send personnel to participate. The draft was completed within a week. The Guangzhou City Chamber of Commerce also formulated proposals to improve the stamp duty law due to the current stamp duty law's harshness and illness to the people.

A proposal to be submitted to the National Industry and Commerce Conference. The original text is as follows: I think that stamp duty is a national tax revenue. If it is handled properly, merchants should sincerely obey it. However, those who carry out inspections are not for promotion but for fines. Whenever they arrive at a store, they are aggressive and

Wolves and tigers watch for flaws and pick bones in eggs. They only know how to use their emotions and do not base fines on laws and regulations, enriching themselves without regard for the

People's pain. If this is the case, then the incompetence of the inspectors is indeed a serious problem.

Seeing this, our association proposed several matters to be improved. If they can be put into practice, it may not be a blessing to the people. (1) Inspectors should wear uniforms and badges to show their marks and show seriousness. At the beginning of the implementation of the stamp law, the original rules stipulated that all inspectors should wear uniforms and badges on their chests, but they were soon

Time and abandoned without use. It is appropriate to restore the old system to prevent abuse and avoid harassment. This should be improved

One (2) Judgment should be allowed to be viewed by the people so as not to be at a loss

Comply. It is found that each branch only issues a ticket notice when executing fines for stamps, and does not state the reasons for the case. When inquiring in the district, they are not allowed to do so. It is appropriate to make a judgment based on the original rules and allow the people to come to the district to view

Those who do not agree may appeal within three days to avoid injustice

Depressed and subsidized compliance. This should be improved. Two (3) Light penalties should be imposed for missed signatures on stamps. Merchants who affix stamps have complied with the rules. If they miss a signature, it is understandable. If they prevent flipping

Affixing, then the penalty for flipping affixing is very severe and can be punished according to the law. It is appropriate to impose light penalties to show leniency and show submission. This should be improved. Three (4) Strictly prohibit the sealing of safes. The stamp duty regulations stipulate that without special orders, one may not tilt boxes, pour baskets, or seal safes. However, recently, when inspectors go to stores for inspection,

If the owner or colleagues are out and the safe cannot be opened without a key,

A sudden seal is added, resulting in all kinds of stagnation and inconvenience. This should be improved. Four. The above four points are hereby proposed for improvement to prevent harshness and show compassion. Whether it is appropriate, please decide publicly (September 8th).

The Mysterious Case of the Infant Corpse: Mrs. Liu Cha, residing at No. 3 Banxian Lane, Jingde Road, Xinmen, adopted a two-year-old boy through Deng Jinsheng and Mrs. Shi Qi in the eleventh month of the lunar calendar last year, paying twenty yuan. Qiantai Cheng Timber Merchant in Xumen was robbed by criminals led by Wei Zhihe on February 19th of this year at 8 PM. The robbers stole $932 in cash and $0.54 in small change. A Case of Fermented Bean Curd 77

Li Xiushan, residing at No. 62 Dataping Lane, Suzhou, knew Li Xuanting when he was a regiment commander in Nanchong, and Li Xuanting was serving in the army in Yunnan. Now, Li Xuanting has also settled in Suzhou at No. 133 Shiquan Street and changed his business to fermented bean curd. On April 26th of this year, Li Xiushan purchased 6,153 catties of fermented bean curd from Li Xuanting, packed in 170 kerosene cans, for a total price of 840 yuan. The goods were shipped from Huqiu to Beijing and then to Nansuzhou, Anhui, for sale. It was agreed that the payment would be made after the goods were sold. Li Xuanting sent Li Zhengxuan and Dai Yun to Nansuzhou to monitor Li Xiushan's sales. After arriving at the destination on May, they saw that the goods were selling well and colluded with Luo Tingbiao, a special agent of the 7th Division stationed there, to seize the goods and sell them for 2,400 yuan (12 yuan per can). After deducting the original cost, there was a profit of 1,200 yuan. Li Xiushan believes that this profit should belong to him, so he hired lawyer Lu Xiangru to sue in the Wuxian District Court to recover the money.

The Dragon Queen Makes a Scene at a Funeral 80

Xue Fengjie, a resident of Xueqian Street in Wuxi, was once a magistrate during the late Qing Dynasty and had only one eye, hence the nickname "Blind Magistrate". Last year, Xue had an affair with Wang Ruiying (nicknamed "Dragon Queen"), the wife of Pang Xueming, the owner of a certain drugstore, and spent $2,700 to help Ruiying divorce her husband and take her as a concubine. They rented a house in the West Drum Tower Lane and lived together. Two months ago, Magistrate Feng suddenly contracted a heart and dropsy disease. Although he sought medical treatment, it was ineffective. He died the other day. The Dragon Queen then hired lawyer Wu Yintang to demand from the Xue family one hundred thousand yuan in living expenses and a city house worth five thousand yuan that Magistrate Feng had promised her before his death. As a result, there was no resolution. Yesterday was the third day of mourning, and the Dragon Queen, with a white turban on her head, wearing a hemp dress and grass shoes, and a hemp rope around her waist, went to pay her respects. Upon arriving at the Xue residence, she cried and made a great scene in the mourning hall, creating chaos.

Seeing that the situation was not good, the Xue family enlisted the help of lawyers Wang Chengzhong and Wu Yintang to negotiate. They asked Lawyer Wu to persuade the Dragon Queen to return home temporarily for further discussion on the settlement of living expenses. The Dragon Queen was satisfied and stopped crying and went home. It is said that the Xue family has agreed to pay her over one thousand yuan in living expenses, which is expected to be resolved in the coming days.

Changzhou 81

Arrest of Bandit Yuan Linfang 82

Liu Yuanshan, captain of the Second Squad of the First Company of the police team stationed in Xiasu, Wuyi County, received a tip that Yuan Linfang and other well-known bandits were in Yuanjia Village. On the night of the 9th, at 12:00 midnight, he led the police team disguised and arrested the bandit Yuan Linfang on the spot, along with a suspect named Gao Jinxiang. After a preliminary hearing, the bandit confessed to joining a certain party and serving as a communication officer. He admitted to being involved in the murder of Jing Peiyin in Danyang in early March of last year, the shooting of Wo Shengfu, and the robbery of the homes of Qi Qianlin and Cao Jifu. Captain Liu obtained the confession and handed him over to the headquarters in the city on the 11th, and then to the county government on the 12th for interrogation.

Financial Panic in Government Agencies 83

The Wuyi County Assets Office believes that the county budget is being fraudulently reported, resulting in a significant deficit. It has specifically sent a letter to the county government requesting that it quickly raise funds to make up for the deficit. County Magistrate Wu proposed this for discussion at the county government meeting on the 11th. The result of the discussion was that, starting in September, the funds for the Public Security Bureau police team would be temporarily reduced to 80%, and the funds for various government agencies and organizations would be temporarily reduced to 50%. Funds will be supplemented as soon as they are available. The method of making up for the deficit will be resolved by a meeting convened by the county government. All government agencies were greatly alarmed upon hearing this news.

Nantong 84

Post-Disaster Arrangement of Bandit Trouble in Huainan Salt Reclamation Area 85

After the districts of Shan Hua Cheng Da Wang, He De He Shun, Ou Geng, Da Sheng Tong, etc. were disturbed by Ma Yu Ren colluding with local bandits and suffered huge losses, Ma still entrenched himself in various districts of the West Pond. With the cotton season in full swing, the representatives of the reclamation decided to first organize local militias to protect the tenant farmers in harvesting cotton. At the same time, they jointly raised 40,000 yuan to purchase equipment and organize a joint reclamation police force. The matter has been submitted to the provincial government for approval, and Xiong Yanghe, the police chief of Funing County, has been entrusted to recruit and train personnel.

Bandits Rampant Again in Eastern Townships 86

The remnants of the bandits in the San Yi Yu and other districts in the eastern townships of Nantong are currently gathering and severing more than a dozen sections of the road, destroying many bridges. The bandits openly occupy civilian fields and harvest cotton and rice.

Anyone who resists is brutally murdered, along with their entire family. The bandit leader, surnamed Cai, is a middle school graduate. The bandit lair is in the area of Xinhe Harbor. According to the telegrams from District Chief Jiang and others, the county government has requested Li Changjiang, the commander of the Jiangbei Bandit Suppression, to lead troops to suppress the bandits and recover the issue of the Langbing Yamen. The Ministry of Military Affairs has ordered the Nantong County Government to recover the former Langshan Military Headquarters, which was occupied by Hai Shan. County Magistrate Zhang stated that the case involves judicial matters and has specifically requested that it be handed over to the county court for execution.

Gaoyou 87

Village Head Accused of Harboring Bandits 88

Dong Moumou, the leader of Sangshuling Township in the county, is currently being accused by Dong Moumou and others from the same township for allegedly allowing the notorious bandit Chen Lazi and others to have a banquet at his home a few days ago. A joint petition has been submitted to the county government requesting that the case be strictly investigated.

Danyang 89

Execution of a Communist Leader 90

Zhu Jinhai, a well-known communist in the county, was captured by the police team and sent to the county for trial for assembling a crowd to rob the families of Shi Shunying in Shijia Village and Zhou Juting in Datun Village, and for injuring the victims. He confessed to the crimes without hesitation. The county government telegraphed the province for approval to execute him.

At 8:00 AM on the morning of the 11th, County Magistrate Shen had the criminal brought out, tied up, and taken to the execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Recent News on Bandits in the Western Townships 91

The bandit situation is rampant in the western townships of Danyang County, which borders Zhenjiang County. It is now heard that this group of bandits has fled to the area of Shigulongwang Temple on the border of Zhenjiang County, demanding the surrender of guns and ammunition and cash from the local militia, and forcing farmers to pay additional taxes. They then fled to Baitu Town, Zhenjiang County. The Zhenjiang Town Public Security Bureau and the local militia fought against the bandits but were defeated and retreated. The bandits then looted and burned the town, causing heavy losses. Now the bandits have fled from Baitu to Liuzhuang Village. The village is close to Jiuli Town in Danyang County, and the defenses are under pressure. County Magistrate Shen has dispatched a police team to defend the area and has telegraphed the province for troops. It is now heard that the Sixth Division of Infantry has been sent from the province, along with the security brigade and the police teams of various counties, to encircle and attack the bandits. The bandits have fled to the area of Maoshan in Zhenjiang County.

Yangzhou 92

Repeated Abduction and Rape, Sent for Investigation 93

Yu Jian, who runs a bamboo shop in Dinggou Town, Seventh District of this county, had his sister introduced to Shen Yonggui, who also works in the same trade, as his wife. The wedding was scheduled for the tenth day of the sixth lunar month of this year. However, before the wedding, his daughter had an affair with Wang Chonglin, who runs a sesame cake shop in the town. The two parties agreed to elope before the wedding. Shen went to Fanchuan to search for her and brought her back. She was still married to Shen and taken to Shanghai to live. However, his daughter was abducted by Wang and Wang's friends, Wang Changfu and Liu Wuhua.

Shen received the news from Shanghai and immediately returned to Ding. He asked around for her whereabouts and reported to the Seventh Sub-Bureau of Public Security. On the other day, she and her lover were arrested in Yangjiazhuang, Shaobo, and brought to the bureau. She has now been escorted to the city and sent to the General Bureau of Public Security for legal action.

Dispute After Huge Sum of Money Found in Corpse 94

Yang Jianwen (from Huai'an), a landlord outside the Dongguan Gate of this city in Sanmao Temple, made a living selling dried turnips and other salted goods. On the 3rd of this month, he took the Yanghengde small steamer back to Huai'an, carrying $505 in banknotes and cash. It is unknown why, but he fell into the water and drowned while the ship was passing through Hehuatang below Shaobo. The next day, his body floated to the Zhaoguan Dam and was discovered by the local township head, who ordered the fisherman Lu Weikai to retrieve it. According to Lu, ten dollars in banknotes and ten dollars in cash were found near the body. He planned to buy a coffin and arrange for the burial. Yang Jianpeng, the deceased's brother, heard the news in Yangzhou and rushed to the scene to identify the body. He also found $305 in banknotes in the hidden pocket of the deceased. According to the above statements, only $180 of the amount carried was missing. The matter was reported to Xiao Shaoyuan, the chief of the Eighth Sub-Bureau of Public Security in Shaobo, who sent police officers to arrest Yang Jianpeng, the deceased's brother, and Lu Weikai, who recovered the body. Yang was considered to be pretending to be a relative in order to obtain the money, and Lu was assumed to have embezzled the missing amount. Although Yang and Lu were proven to be who they said they were, it was ineffective. It is said that Yang and Lu have been detained in the bureau for nine days.

Therefore, Yang has asked several colleagues to write a document reporting to the General Bureau of Public Security to prove that he is not pretending to be a relative and requesting that the sub-bureau be ordered to release them. After hearing the news, Chief Xiao of the sub-bureau escorted Yang and Lu to the city yesterday (the 10th) and handed them over to the General Bureau of Public Security for punishment.

County Meetings to Manage Acreage Tax 95

The transfer of towns for the Jiangbei Canal Project has been reported previously. Due to the lack of knowledge of the reorganization of the office and the discovery of many publications exposing the contents of the office and raising questions about the reorganization, the people of each county are suspicious. Bao held a meeting in Yangzhou on the 10th to discuss the management of acreage taxes. As a result, it was divided into two categories: (1) seek the consent of those involved in each county; (2) request a meeting of councillors to clarify the truth about the reorganization.

Using Grain Tax to Offset Customs Bonds 96

The county government received a telegram from the Finance Department requesting that it use the extra $2 per item allowed for winter grain to offset the shortage of the 19th-year Customs Short-Term Treasury Bonds, with half of the amount to be submitted first. It jointly sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce on the 11th to discuss the offsetting method at 2 PM in the county council hall.

Qingjiang 97

Fierce Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits in Yugou 98

Since the town of Yugou in the Fourth District of Huaiyin was captured by bandits on the 22nd of last month, hundreds of people have been kidnapped at once, making it difficult to redeem them all. On the night of the 7th, more than a dozen bandits sneaked into Yugou to collect ransoms (i.e., urge the victims to redeem the kidnapped people). The cavalry of the 7th Company of the 266th Regiment of the official army stationed in the town and the police brigade stationed in Yugou discovered this and immediately divided up to intercept and suppress them. The bandits actually resisted arrest until dawn. The bandits were injured five or six people and retreated, while it was reported that the soldiers were also injured one soldier.

Changshu 99

Director and Manager Reported for Opium Case 100

Hao Bingzhang, the new director of the Finance Bureau of this county, and Hao Shebo, the manager of the Bank of China, are cousins. Director Hao came to Changshu to take office only two days ago. On the evening of the 10th, at about 11:00 PM, Director Hao met with Hao Shebo at his home to discuss important matters. Xu Junda, a resident of Nanmen, learned that Hao Shebo had an opium addiction and knew that the new Director Hao also had this addiction. He reported to the First Sub-Station and led the arrest by patrol officer Luo Qifan of the sub-station. Xu first knocked on the door of Hao Shebo's house at No. 22 Caodang and then entered with the police officer to search. Eleven opium certificates were found. At that time, Director Hao was already guarded by the police officer and Xu.

Hao Shebo said, "Today I am willing to sign a certificate and go to the bureau with him for questioning tomorrow." Director Hao was able to escape. Later, Cheng Shaoxiang, the mayor of Siqian Town, arrived after Hao Shebo's telegram request for consultation for a long time. Cheng went to the Public Security Bureau to provide temporary bail. On the morning of the 11th, Patrol Officer Luo of the sub-station sent the seized opium certificates and the informant's certificate to the General Bureau. Hao Shebo also submitted a sick report to the General Bureau requesting exemption from summons. Wang, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, sent the sub-station's report and the defendant's sick report to the county government. In the afternoon, Cen Hongzhi, the trial member of the county government, ordered the informant Xu Junda to be interrogated alone and ordered him to await investigation. It is said that Director Hao had an audience with County Magistrate Tan on the night of the incident and requested that the county government send him to the hospital for examination.

Jiashan 101

Bandit Suppression in Qingpu Flees into Zhejiang Province 102

The other day, over fifty bandit ships in the area of Xiaozheng Fanbang New Town, Qingpu, were discovered by the Jiangsu Provincial Resident Water Police. They organized and encircled and suppressed them. The bandits relied on their stubborn resistance, and both sides opened fire in a fierce battle for three hours. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and fled in the direction of Zhuangqiao Fengjing, Jiashan, Zhejiang Province. It is estimated that eight or nine were killed, more than ten were injured, and five were captured alive and sent to Qing for legal action. Upon receiving the report, preparations have been made separately for prevention. Four kidnapped people from Tianning returned. It was learned yesterday that seven people were kidnapped in the Tianning robbery case. After the bandits kidnapped each ticket, they separately questioned the family and sent bandits to investigate. Those who were proved to be poor were released. Two more, surnamed Pan and Lu, had to be redeemed at a good price. The ticket for the woman has been torn up.

Huzhou 103

Fierce Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits Under the Moonlight in Si'an Town 104

Suddenly, on the 9th, a large group of over 500 bandits with submachine guns, Mauser pistols, and other weapons were discovered hiding just a mile from Si'an Town, Changxing County, Huzhou. Fortunately, the Third Battalion of the Second Regiment of the Security Team stationed in Si'an was aware of this. The battalion dispatched troops to defend the area and telegraphed the headquarters of the Second Regiment in the city. Regiment Commander Jiao, upon hearing the news, immediately led a machine gun company to the scene to join the Third Battalion in suppressing the bandits. Seeing that a large army had arrived, the bandits prepared to resist arrest. The two sides exchanged fire fiercely under the moonlight for a long time. The army used machine guns to sweep forward, and the bandits were unable to withstand the attack and retreated. It is said that they fled towards Guangde County in Anhui Province.

Kidnapping Case in Lu's Family in Yujiadian 105

On the late night of the 8th, eight or nine bandits suddenly came to Lu A'er's home in Yujiadian, a place three miles away from Nanhao Bridge in the northern township of this city. Each of them was armed with guns and weapons, broke through the back wall and entered.

A'er heard the noise and hid first. His thirteen-year-old son was unable to escape and was kidnapped by the bandits. All the clothes and silver dollars in his house were robbed, with an estimated loss of about 200 yuan. Before leaving, the bandits fired several shots as a warning and kidnapped Lu A'er's son.

Pinghu 106

Complications in the Inheritance Issue of the Lu Family 107

Ji Shi, the wife of the late Lu Libin in the Lotus Pond in the southern city of this county, died of illness on the 10th of this month at the age of 67. Ji had a daughter, Lu Yulin, who married Cheng Daizhong of Nanhetou in the 14th year of the Republic of China (both husband and wife work in the education sector). Usually, the couple lives in the Lu residence. Recently, because her mother was seriously ill, Yulin moved all her property away. Zhou Jia, the maternal nephew of the deceased and a lawyer, heard about this and instigated Lu Yulin, saying that a woman has the right of inheritance. So, on the one hand, he published a statement in the newspaper, and on the other hand, he designed to prevent the great-grandson Lu Chengqing and his wife from entering the house for mourning. Zhou Jia also came forward himself, secretly colluding with hooligans and inviting the patrol officer of the Sixth Precinct to help drive them out. By the time the sacrificial great-grandson arrived, Lu Lanbo, the clan leader of the Lu family, came forward to reason with him. Zhou

Jia, the lawyer (from Jiaxing), became even more agitated. The clan leader asked him to file a lawsuit in the county, but he refused. At that time, many onlookers were angered and almost took him to the county to be dealt with by obstructing the funeral. Seeing that the situation was not good, the police officers realized that they had been deceived by Zhou and apologized to the clan leader of the Lu family. Lawyer Zhou saw that he was unreasonable and ran away. The Lu family was then allowed to perform the funeral on time.

Planning to Build Civilian Housing in Various Counties 109

In recent years, the Zhejiang Construction Department has seen an increase in the province's population and a scarcity of housing, resulting in landlords charging exorbitant rents and various forms of oppression. In order to solve the plight of tenants, it is planning to build dozens of civilian houses in each county and rent them out at a fair price. The construction costs will be allocated from local public funds, and all construction matters will be overseen by the County Assets Committee.

The Zhejiang Relief Association has already finalized the distribution of 10,000 yuan of Zhejiang Relief Public Bonds issued in this province. (1) Approximately 130,000 yuan will be used to redeem the public bonds issued for the dismissal and salary reduction. (2) Approximately 111,000 yuan will be issued to various counties for relief. (3) Approximately 200,000 yuan will be sent to the Finance Department to raise cash and repay loans. (4) Approximately 145,000 yuan will be allocated to the Hua Yang Relief balance to issue the public bonds. (5) Over 200,000 yuan will be deposited in various banks to offset cash and repay loans. The above totals over 780,000 yuan, with over 90,000 yuan remaining.

Ningbo 111

Revolt of Prisoners in Fenghua is Shocking News 112

Yesterday (around 5:00 PM on the 10th), over a hundred inmates in the Fenghua County Prison suddenly revolted, led by Guan Rongjing, a murderer who had been sentenced to life imprisonment, and Cai Dian, Du Wu, Zhou Zhong, Wu Rongsheng, and four other thieves. Prior to the revolt, the inmates took advantage of the prison guards' lack of vigilance and used kitchen knives, firewood, wine, porcelain, and other items as weapons to break through the prison doors and swarm out. The prison guards were caught off guard, resulting in the escape of 68 inmates. Police officer Lu Naiwu and guard Chen Haijie were seriously injured. Upon hearing the alarm, the security team stationed near the county government immediately dispatched many members to encircle and arrest the escapees. One escapee was killed on the spot, and another was killed by the security team after escaping through the back door of the prison to Sandi. In addition, Sun Jintai, a thief who stole from Sun Biaoqing's house in Xiaowang Temple in Qianyu, was shot in the left leg. As a result, only three escapees were captured: Wang Lianghua, Li Jizong, and Xia Amao. The rest have fled far away. County Magistrate Zhu Maoqi considered that the negligent behavior of Warden Hong Jinqi

led to this disaster and had him arrested. The injured police officer Lu Naiwu and others have been sent to the County Hospital for treatment.

250,000 Loan Still Awaiting Discussion 113

Regarding the provincial government's proposal to borrow 250,000 yuan from the silver and money industries in this city, it is now heard that provincial special envoy Zhu Luzhong convened leaders from the silver and money industries at the Chamber of Commerce yesterday to discuss the matter. For this loan, they verbally promised to add 10,000 yuan from the unified tax on foreign goods in addition to the shipping license tax. It is said that Zhang Jifu and other leaders from the silver and money industries agreed to reply after discussing the matter with their colleagues.

Collision of Steamships Injures People 114

At 3:00 PM the other day (the 9th), the Dongxing steamship of the Southeast Steamship Company of this city was near the Xinliang Pavilion of Panhuo Bridge when it was suddenly hit by the Ninghu steamship of the Ninghu Company. The second-class towboat was broken and sunk, and passengers Wang and Yuan were injured. They were immediately sent to Puyi Hospital in Mozhiyan for treatment. Afterwards, the Southeast Company has filed a complaint with the relevant authorities.

Local News

Inauguration of Shanghai-Sichuan Aviation 115

Yesterday morning, the Chongqing branch of China National Aviation Corporation commenced trial flights on the Shanghai-Chongqing air route. The aircraft used was the company's own "Jiujiang" Loening amphibious aircraft. The company's inaugural ceremony procedures were finalized yesterday as seven items: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party Song; (3) Salute the National Flag; (4) Pay the highest respect to the portrait of the Premier; (5) Respectfully read the Testament; (6) All staff

bow once to the new Director; (7) Director's address. (Photographed).

After the ceremony, national flags were hung above the main and side entrances of the bureau yesterday.

Notice to staff: Today is the inauguration of the new Director, and all staff within the bureau must be present to welcome him. The administrative section widely distributed notices yesterday, informing all staff and heads of various departments to be present this morning.

Preparations for the Jiujiang's trial flight to Chongqing. (Photo by this newspaper).

The Jiujiang's departure for its trial flight to Chongqing.

The chief and deputy directors of the aviation team, Mr. Smith and Mr. Nie Kaiyi, piloted the aircraft from the Longhua seaplane base at 8:15 AM yesterday.

The company's vice chairman, Hamilton, also accompanied them. Half an hour before the trial flight, the pilot started the engine to test it for about twenty minutes. Necessary supplies were also placed in the aircraft. At that time, the "Shanghai" aircraft heading to Hankou had already prepared passengers and mail after the bell rang eight times, and departed first. The "Jiujiang" aircraft for the trial flight to Chongqing was then pushed onto the dock. Fifteen minutes later, the pilots and others boarded the aircraft one after another, and the sound of the engine rattled. The aircraft accelerated from slow to fast, skimming across the water and

taking off quickly into the sky. The long journey of more than 3,600 li thus began. The success of the future Shanghai-Chengdu aviation enterprise greatly depends on the success of this trial flight. The aircraft must land and stay briefly in Nanjing and Jiujiang. It is scheduled to arrive in Hankou in the afternoon yesterday, stay overnight in Hankou, and continue to fly to Yichang this morning. It will fly to Wanxian tomorrow morning and arrive in Chongqing next Monday, stay overnight, and fly directly back to Hankou from Chongqing on Tuesday, and fly back to Shanghai on Wednesday. A direct flight from Shanghai to Chongqing without stopping can be achieved in twelve hours. This trial flight requires four days because of the detailed survey of the terrain along the way. After the official flight next month, the Shanghai-Hankou route will still have one round trip per day, each trip taking seven hours. The Hankou-Chongqing route will have one round trip per week in the initial phase, each trip taking eight hours. The new American aircraft delivered on the 19th of this month will be used exclusively for the Hankou-Chongqing route, while the original aircraft will still be used for the Shanghai-Hankou route. The Shanghai-Hankou route will still use Jingxun as landing stations, while the Hankou-Chongqing route will use the newly established Yiwan as landing stations. Passengers and mail can get on and off at each station.

Li Zhonggong Takes Office as Director of China Merchants Bureau This Morning 116

Cai Pei went to Nanjing last night. Li Zhonggong, the new director of the China Merchants Bureau, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing and has been residing at No. 200 Avenue Road. After contacting various parties recently, it has been approved that he will formally take office at the bureau at 10:00 AM today. The details of the handover are recorded as follows:

Inauguration ceremony: Director Li has scheduled to formally take office at the bureau this morning. Zhou Shian, acting head of the administrative section, ordered the establishment of an auditorium on the second floor of the bureau. It was decorated yesterday afternoon, filled with national flags. In the center of the podium is the portrait of the Premier.

Mr. Li Zhonggong 117

At nine o'clock, all staff must gather in the bureau. When the new Director arrives, all staff will welcome him in front of the auditorium, and the heads of various departments and secretaries will be sent to the front door of the bureau to greet Mr. Li upstairs to the chairman's seat. Yesterday afternoon, the administrative section of the bureau also sent a letter to the police station requesting them to send officers to the bureau to ensure solemnity. As for the staff of the bureau

participating in the welcome, each person will be issued a badge for identification.

Anyone without this badge will not be allowed to enter.

Declaration outline: Today, when Mr. Li takes office, he will prepare to announce a declaration personally written on the reorganization of the bureau's affairs. The declaration is very long, divided into six paragraphs. First, it states the reason for taking office is due to the government's urging, which cannot be refused. Secondly, it describes the past of the China Merchants Bureau and concludes. Thirdly, it describes the reasons for reorganization and the authority to reorganize. Fourth, it describes the criteria for hiring people, adopting talent-based principles.

The declaration was sent to the bureau by Mr. Li around 3:00 PM yesterday and handed over to the administrative section for copying and mimeographing, to be directly distributed to various newspapers today for publication. The most important point in the declaration is to reveal that the major power of the bureau's affairs will belong to the reorganization committee established later. The future methods of the China Merchants Bureau, whether state-owned or commercial, state-managed or still commercially operated, will all be decided by the reorganization committee through public discussion. It is said that all major matters of the bureau's reorganization staff are determined by the reorganization committee, and the Director is only an administrative agency executing the resolutions of the reorganization committee. Cai Pei, the outgoing representative of the Director, Cai Ziping, came to Shanghai to take over for more than a week. Because the new appointment has been determined, Mr. Cai visited Mr. Li's residence yesterday to hand over all the bureau's affairs. Therefore, he left the bureau yesterday. From today, he will go to the bureau again. Cai had been away from Nanjing for a long time.

The official business in the department is very busy. It is said that he resigned from Mr. Li yesterday and took the evening train to Nanjing to resume his original position as Director of the Navigation Administration Department.

Determination of the Constructor of the Premier's Bronze Statue 119

As a result of the bidding, Jiang Xiaojian was selected. The Construction Committee of the Premier's Bronze Statue of All Circles in Shanghai held its sixth plenary meeting in the Road Bureau conference room yesterday afternoon.

Important issues were decided. Committee members Wang Xiaolai, Ye Huijun, Zheng Chengqing, Wang Binyan, Ye Xiufu, and others attended the meeting. Two models of the Premier's face were displayed at the meeting, but the makers were not identified to ensure fairness. The meeting then opened for discussion, and Wang Xiaolai was publicly elected as chairman to discuss the following results: (1) Discuss the proposal of whether Li Jinfa's model can participate. It was resolved that models without submitted drawings and photos would not be allowed to participate. (2) Discuss which model to adopt. Three Overseas Chinese Compatriots from the Netherlands Were Expelled and Returned to China 120

Propagating Party principles was envied. The Overseas Chinese Association is scheduled to welcome them. Yesterday, three overseas Chinese compatriots who had been deported from Xilibo Island, Wangjiaxi port, returned to China. One was Mr. Liao Peizhi, the editor-in-chief of the local Chinese newspaper "Minsheng Bao," one was Ms. Pan Fengjing, a teacher at the Zhongshan Public School in the local Party office, who was hired by the Central Training Department, and one was Ms. Chen Zhongshu, who was introduced by the Cultural Affairs Department of Jinan University to the local Chinese school. They took the Dutch Java Company's mail ship Zhijinpeng to Xiamen and transferred to the Chinese ship Changan, arriving in Shanghai on the 9th. They were introduced by Mr. Liu Shimu to the local Overseas Chinese Federation and talked to the committee members about their experience of being expelled. The reasons for the expulsion are recorded below. Mr. Liao has been serving in the education and newspaper circles in Nanyang for many years, holding a spirit of fearless confrontation with Dutch imperialists. Last year, he returned to Java and edited the "Daily Telegraph" to Wangjiaxi, where he edited the Party newspaper to promote the Three People's Principles, promote overseas Chinese community culture, and advocate the national salvation movement, all using his sharp pen to make powerful appeals. Therefore, it aroused the jealousy of the Dutch Indian government, and they were always picking on the words published in the newspapers, fabricating crimes and adding accusations. The court illegally sentenced him to fines repeatedly, but Mr. Liao never succumbed and thoroughly implemented his spirit of upholding justice and righteousness, which made the Dutch imperialists even more fearful, so they used their highest means of oppression to order deportation. The most regrettable thing is that Mr. Liao was planning to expand the "Min Bao" and had made considerable progress, but he suddenly suffered this setback and failed to achieve his wishes, which is a major loss to the overseas Chinese news community. It is heard that the position of editor-in-chief has now been taken over by Mr. Chen Guan of the Central Propaganda Department, who is going to take over. What is hoped of Mr. Chen is that he will undertake the mission of the central government, continue Mr. Liao's unfinished business, and save the overseas Chinese from their increasingly declining

crisis. As for Ms. Pan and Ms. Chen, they recently arrived in Wangjiaxi from Shanghai for less than a month. Their entry procedures were very complete, but they were inexplicably deported by the Dutch imperialists with an order without even announcing the reasons. If this is the case, then overseas Chinese will have no place to stand in overseas. This kind of tyrannical behavior by the Dutch imperialists is not a personal issue, but a destruction of international relations and an uncivilized act. I don't know how our country's diplomatic authorities will solve the plight of millions of overseas Chinese. Mr. Liao and others also recounted the humiliation they suffered from the Dutch imperialists before leaving the country, which made people hear it with hair standing on end and tears falling. I write this to tell the Chinese people, what should they think? The committee members of the Overseas Chinese Federation believe that Mr. Liao and others have sacrificed for the country and have suffered dust from afar to return, and will hold a meeting to welcome them.

Japan Orders Quarantine 121

Another Difficulty for Passengers Going to Japan: Japan is preparing for the autumn military exercises. Recently, the country has been particularly strict on domestic health and epidemic prevention, and has paid great attention to foreign

ships. During this strict prevention, a floating corpse was suddenly found on the Japanese sea. After the customs medical officer and others went to verify it, it was determined that it was a crew member or sailor on a ship to Japan who died of an epidemic and was thrown into the sea. Since this incident, the Japanese authorities have issued a maritime alert order, designating that any ship from Shanghai, Tianjin, Qingdao, or other Chinese ports to Japan that goes to ports such as Kobe, Nagasaki, and Moji will be ordered to implement quarantine for passengers to prevent the spread of epidemics.

The quarantine method is to order each ship to issue wax boxes to passengers when they board the ship to collect passenger feces and send them to the importing customs doctor for chemical verification. If there is an epidemic, they will not be allowed to land and will be quarantined. All ships from Shanghai to Japan will also implement this. From now on, it will be very difficult for Chinese people to go to Japan.

County Public Security Expenses for August Have Been Secured 122

The Crisis of China's Tung Oil Trade 123

The Consulate in Penang reports that tung oil is a unique product of China, but in recent years, the United States has advocated planting to resist it. The former Consul-General in New York of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs reported on the current situation and prospects of Chinese tung oil in the United States, arousing the attention of domestic industrial circles. Subsequently, the ministry, based on the report from the Consulate in Penang on the crisis of China's tung oil trade, which is sufficient for political reference, has sent a letter to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to copy the original document to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Inspection Bureau for reference. The original report is recorded as follows:

According to the investigation, Sichuan and Guangdong tung oil is a purely Chinese product. In the past, it was only used for waterproofing houses, boats, utensils, etc., and its value was not very high. Recently, with the increasing use of this material in the aircraft industry, electrical industry, and other industries, exports have increased and the value has risen. According to the latest survey, annual exports reach 30 million yuan, ranking third among China's export goods. The largest sales market is the United States. The varnish it produces initially used flaxseed oil, but it is not as dense and suitable as tung oil and is easy to dry, so they have adopted China's

tung oil. However, China is completely using manual extraction and has no fixed standards, so the products are often of varying quality. After being transported to the United States, factories must re-

chemically verify and refine it, which has led them to develop their own strategies for planting tung oil trees. It is heard that the US government has allocated 50 million yuan in Florida to try planting in the largest area. It is expected that it can be harvested in 25 years, then the Chinese tung oil trade will suffer a major blow. What's more, in the South Seas, due to the drop in rubber and coconut prices, the British authorities have proposed planting tung oil trees, then the danger of our country's tung oil in trade is even greater. Because of the relationship between strains, Malaya is most suitable for agricultural operations. Therefore, the rain and dew are all over the territory. However, in recent years, the price of rubber has fallen and the price of coconut has also fallen. Those who are engaged in this business are suffering endlessly. According to the London Telegraph on July 16, the British Products Association's Building Trade Department has been trying to plant tung oil in Malaya, India, Africa, and the West Indies, and will be able to achieve results. The current results of the trials in British territories are still

uncertain, but according to reports from various places, there seem to be good results, especially in northeastern India. If the trial planting is successful, then in the future, the position of our country's important goods in trade will be taken over by foreigners. In recent years, our country's foreign trade position in the international arena has been extremely backward. Today, foreigners are not only engaging in aggression against our country's economy, but also launching fundamental attacks. The future is dangerous and we are shivering with fear. Only if our government informs the industrialists can they be prepared for a rainy day.

A Written Statement from the Chinese Merchants' Straw Hat Export Industry 124

The Yushang Hat Manufacturing Company, a member of the Chinese Merchants' Straw Hat Export Industry Association, runs a straw hat factory in Yuyao, which is sold abroad and has long been exempted from taxes by the ministry. Recently, the local straw hat donation bureau has been forcibly collecting donations, causing disputes that have not been resolved for a long time. The company has submitted a request to the Zhejiang Finance Department to clarify the matter, as follows: In order to comply with the overseas donation exemption method for overseas straw hats, we are willing to provide a corresponding guarantee and request that the Zhejiang Provincial Export Straw Hat Donation Collection Office in Shaoxing follow the procedures. Our company collects and transports straw hats exclusively for sale overseas. According to the ministry's order, all donations are exempted. We have submitted a request to your department to request that the precedent be followed. We have received your approval No. 218, stating that the overseas straw hat donation exemption method was previously ordered by the Ministry of Finance and has been notified to all bureaus for compliance. If the company's straw hats are indeed sold abroad, they should be exempted from donations in accordance with the overseas straw hat donation exemption method, without the need for separate notification. I hope you will know and attach the approval for temporary storage, etc. Unexpectedly, the Zhejiang Provincial Straw Hat Donation Collection Office in Shaoxing does not comply with the laws and regulations, claiming that they have not received the notification or know the donation exemption method, etc., extorting donations and obstructing transportation, which not only endangers industry and commerce but also disregards the ministry's and your department's orders. Such harsh donations and taxes are not the national intention to protect merchants and benefit the people. For this reason, we submit a request to order the collection office to follow the donation exemption method proposed by the Ministry of Finance and not to unreasonably obstruct it. In the future, if straw hats are exported overseas, our company will provide a corresponding guarantee in accordance with the precedents in Ningbo, Haimen, and other places. Once the export form is received from the Jianghai Customs, the guarantee will be verified and canceled to comply with the ministry's order and maintain commerce. I beg you to issue a prompt notification to all straw hat donation collection offices to comply, which is for the public convenience. Respectfully presented to the Zhejiang Finance Department.

General Rules for Issuing Permits for People's Organizations 125

Page 14

The People's Training Committee of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang received today from the Central Training Department the General Rules for Issuing Permits for People's Organizations and has issued a special notice to the people of the city to comply. The original text is recorded as follows: In order to notify the case, the Central Executive Committee Training Department ordered the issuance of the General Rules for Issuing Permits for People's Organizations to be promulgated to the public so that everyone may know this notice. September 13, 19th year of the Republic of China. The General Rules for Issuing Permits for People's Organizations are as follows: Article 1 These general rules are formulated in accordance with the People's Organization Organization Plan. Article 2 Provincial (Special City) and County (City) Party Departments and Special Party Departments shall issue permits for people's organizations in accordance with these general rules. Article 3 After the Party Department accepts the application for permission to organize from the organizers of a people's organization, it shall send personnel to inspect within one week. After reviewing the inspection report and finding it qualified, it may issue a permit. Article 4 The permit for people's organizations may be manufactured and decorated by each Party Department in accordance with the style promulgated by the Central Government. Article 5 If the organizers of a people's organization lose the permit, they shall immediately submit a statement of the reasons for requesting a replacement. Article 6 If the organizers of a people's organization have not prepared the organization within six months after receiving the permit, the original issuing Party Department may revoke the permit. Article 7 The Party Department shall collect stamp duty according to regulations for issuing permits and shall not charge any other handling fees. Article 8 These general rules shall be promulgated and implemented by the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

The Social Bureau Mediated the Sino-Japanese Labor Dispute Yesterday 129

Huadong News Agency reported that the Shanghai Social Bureau summoned representatives from both the labor and capital sides of the Japanese-Chinese yarn factory at the bureau at 9:00 AM yesterday to begin mediating the factory's labor dispute. The mediation situation is divided into the following records:

Attendees: The attendees included Guo Yongxi, director of the mediation section of the Social Bureau, Wang Guoxian, representative of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Zhang Yaoming, representative of the Municipal Party Department, Qian Zhongnan, translator of the Social Bureau, Wang Zhiqin, recorder, Zhao Bi and Yu Qixiang, labor representatives, Tsuji Keisho, chief manager of the general factory, Xi Chuan, representative of the Japanese Yarn Factory Federation, Cao Shiming, translator, and Cao Shunqing, representative of the Fifth District Party Department and Oikawa, head of the personnel section of the Japanese-Chinese yarn factory, as observers.

Mediation situation: After the formal greetings, Chairman Guo first reported the purpose of the mediation and stated the situation of the crossing of the river yesterday, hoping that the representatives of the labor and capital sides would discuss and concede to each other with the utmost sincerity so as not to disappoint the authorities' mediation efforts. The labor representatives then detailed the reasons for the strike and requested that four additional points be added to the three conditions originally proposed to the factory: (1) Workers must be paid for all commemorative festivals promulgated by the central government; (2) Four former members of the labor union flattered the capital and coerced the workers with concrete evidence, and Wu Zhongyue, a company employee, recently impersonated a representative to report to the capital with the intention of sabotaging the labor union. The labor union requested the factory to fire them; (3) The capital insisted on firing seven workers, including Yu Qixiang, for inciting the labor dispute. The labor side believed that there was no such thing as inciting the labor dispute and the factory's dismissal could not be recognized; (4) Wages must be paid during the strike period. Chairman Guo discussed with the capital side. The capital representative said that the first of the original three articles, the increase of rice subsidies of one unit per day, was not recognized; the second article, wages must not be delayed, could be followed; the third article, stopping night work on Sundays, had now agreed that the workers would not raise it because the autumn was cool. As for the four additional conditions, they were considered to be important issues: (1) The holiday issue was not recognized because all Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai did not have this rule, which was related to the entire industry; (2) The capital did not want to fire the five people who were considered running dogs by the labor side because they had no running dog behavior; (3) The capital believed that the seven people including Yu Qixiang did incite the workers and must be fired; (4) Wages during the strike period were too much of a loss and could not be recognized in any way. However, the capital originally rewarded workers with two days of extra work per month as a subsidy for labor losses, but only this time and must be stopped thereafter. It was also stated that the Pudong Japanese-Chinese yarn factory had always treated workers well and there was no oppression. For example, even if there was

a reward of work at other factories, workers would have to deduct it if they stopped working, but this side did not have this problem. The labor representatives immediately refuted, saying that the capital's so-called preferential treatment was just empty talk. Today, it can be used to generally describe the rest, for example, the monthly reward of work in

other Japanese factories is four days per month, but they only have two days, how can they be considered preferential treatment? Therefore, they requested that the chairman add this point to the three conditions and four requests proposed by the labor union in order to increase the monthly reward of work

from two days to four days. At that time, the Japanese side did not make any comments on this, but

repeatedly stated other preferential conditions to the chairman. The chairman repeatedly persuaded them to no avail. At that time, the official representative believed that the two sides were going in opposite directions and were too far apart, believing that it was necessary to mediate separately. Therefore, he ordered the labor representatives to withdraw and discuss with each other on the other side. As a result, the labor side temporarily reserved the rice subsidy issue until the reward of work was resolved. At that time, it was already noon and it was announced that the meeting would be adjourned. At 1:30 PM, the original representatives rejoined the mediation. However, although the labor and capital sides were able to

sincerely discuss each point, the fundamental aspects could not be approached. Therefore, the chairman truthfully told the representatives of both sides to return to the meeting and decide on the possible scope and make sure not to go to extremes, and then convene both sides to mediate again.

Committee for Revising the Constitution of the Red Cross Society 132

Continuing the Meeting The Committee for Revising the Constitution of the Chinese Red Cross Society held its eighth meeting at 2:00 PM on September 11th. Attendees included committee members Li Zhenbang, Wen Lanting, Xu Xichun, Wang Peiyuan, Wu Jiasan, Ye Zhisheng, Dong Biqin, Wang Raolai, Xue Shaoting, and Liu Hongsheng. Secretary Wei Ruifeng recorded the minutes. After the ceremony, the draft agenda was read, and the members raised no objections. The chairman signed it. (1) The chairman reported that the Election Law for Standing Committee Members would be read for the second time today. (1) Committee member Wu Jiasan suggested that Article 12 should be amended to read: "The initial election area shall be the general assembly for members belonging to the general assembly, and each branch for members belonging to branches." The original Article 13 should be amended to read: "The supervisors of the initial election shall be the speaker and deputy speaker, chairman and vice chairman of the general assembly, and the speaker and deputy speaker, chairman and vice chairman of the branch." (1) Committee member Li Zhenbang suggested that Article 14 should read: "The number of elected candidates shall be as follows: (1) One person for every 30 full members; (2) Two persons for every 30 to 100 full and ordinary members; (3) Three persons for every 100 or more full and ordinary members; (4) Four persons for every 500 or more full and ordinary members; (5) Five persons for every 1,000 or more full and ordinary members." Committee member Wu Jiasan suggested adding "but at most ten, and no more than five above." (1) The chairman suggested that Article 15 should be revised in detail. After public discussion, Article 15 was revised to read: "The date of the initial election shall be notified to each branch by the general assembly three months in advance. The general assembly shall also notify all members and appoint a preparatory committee of nine to fifteen people from the Standing Committee to handle all matters related to the general assembly. The detailed rules shall be formulated separately, but preparatory committee members shall not be limited to Standing Committee members." (1) Committee member Wu Jiasan suggested that Article 17 should be amended to read: "After the general assembly receives the list of candidates from the initial election of the branch, it shall stamp the election ballots with the official seal of the association within two weeks." (1) The chairman suggested that "sealed by the speaker of the council" in Article 19 should be changed to "sealed by the speaker and supervisors." (1) Committee member Ye Zhisheng suggested adding "and sent to the preparatory committee of the general assembly" to the end of Article 20. (1) Committee member Wu Jiasan suggested adding a supplementary article: "The amendment of this election law must be passed by more than half of the delegates attending the National Congress of Members," and list it as the second item. (1) The chairman said that the second reading of this election law has been completed. The meeting will continue tomorrow to read the general rules of the association for the second time. The meeting adjourned at a little after 5:00 PM.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Develops Trade with Fiji 137

Preparing for the Fiji Philippine National Products Exhibition

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce instructed the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce: "In order to comply with orders in the case, I have investigated that the Fiji Philippine Carnival Industry and Commerce Exhibition is held in February every year, and I have repeatedly invited our country to participate. In order to develop trade with Fiji, the Ministry has prepared exhibits and sent personnel to participate at the request of the association in the eighteenth year. After the meeting, it was reported that our country's exports were very popular among the people of Fiji, and that there are many overseas Chinese merchants in Fiji who are very hopeful of promoting national products. However, because all the exhibits brought to the meeting were shipped back and returned after the participants returned home, there was still little contact with the operation of trade. It can be seen that the government's dispatch of personnel to the meeting only fulfilled the friendship of the state, and in order to export national products, merchants should be sent to the meeting by themselves. In view of this, the Ministry approved the letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the presentation from the Consul General in Fiji in November and December of last year, inviting the Carnival Industry and Commerce Exhibition to be held this year, and ordered the former Shanghai Merchant Group Consolidation Committee to convene industrial and commercial groups in Shanghai and companies and manufacturers engaged in South Seas exports to participate, and to raise capital and set up a long-term export agency during the meeting in accordance with business methods to develop trade with Fiji. In January of this year, the Merchant Consolidation Committee replied that the meeting period was very tight and the capital was raised to set up an export agency that could not be completed as scheduled and planned to wait for the next session to prepare for participation. It was also approved to discuss and proceed at any time. Now, according to the Consul General of Fiji, Guang Xukun, he presented the association's letter requesting our country to participate in the 1933 Carnival Industry and Commerce Exhibition, and a copy of the English letter was attached to the Ministry in addition to instructions, and an English letter was copied to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce for reference and processing of the previous case. It is still far from the meeting period, and I hope to plan and advance as soon as possible. Also, according to the Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce, it has successively submitted reports to the Shanghai National Products Factory Joint Conference that personnel will be sent to the port to discuss holding a national products mobile exhibition, and the names, addresses, goods, and trademarks of the national products factories should be compiled and distributed to overseas Chinese merchants. The former Shanghai Merchant Group Consolidation Committee has replied by telegram that it has forwarded the notice to the China National Products Maintenance Association and various national products groups for compliance, and has ordered the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inform the silk manufacturers to comply with the case. The Ministry believes that participating in the Fiji Philippine Carnival Industry and Commerce Exhibition and contacting to hold the Singapore National Products Mobile Exhibition are all for promoting national products and seeking to increase exports to the South Seas. Now that gold is expensive and silver is cheap, it is a thousand-year opportunity to expand overseas trade. Since the Shanghai manufacturers have a resolution in front, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which is in a leading position, should take the responsibility of guidance and follow the previous case. When the new port is held, a long-term export agency should be set up to coordinate methods, contact and proceed, so that national products can be sold in the South Seas Islands. The Ministry has high hopes for this order."
