Xuan Aihou Rescued After Being Kidnapped 141

The Bandits Demanded a Ransom of 300,000

The Amount Was Too Large to Negotiate

The Detectives Fought Bravely

A Total of Two Bandits Were Arrested The Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank Trust Department Director Xuan Aihou, a native of Gaoyou, was kidnapped at 8:40 AM on the 2nd of this month in front of his residence at No. 41 Bailainei Montmarang Road in the French Concession. At that time, the bank sent a letter to various newspapers requesting that they not be published temporarily in order to facilitate the investigation and avoid accidents. Therefore, most newspapers did not disclose it the next day. It has been ten days without any progress. It is now reported that the bandit den was discovered by the French patrol room yesterday morning, and the hostages were rescued on the spot, and ten bandits were captured one after another. The details are as follows:

Negotiations at the New World Restaurant After being kidnapped, Xuan's family received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 300,000 gold. The family sent people to secretly contact the bandits several times, and the bandits wanted at least 200,000 yuan. However, because the amount was too large, the negotiations failed. After a long delay, the detectives and inspectors of the special agency of the French patrol room, Jin Jiulin, learned that the bandits were hiding in Room 24 of the New World Hotel in the Public Concession and were waiting for Ling Fang to negotiate. He immediately reported to West Inspector Pei Er and Patrolmen No. 39 West Pei, along with the detectives Li Yaolong, Mao Jingen, Wang Rusong, Qian Yumin, Lu Zhulin, and Bao detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhou Bingcheng, Zhou Buguang, etc., and armed themselves and rushed to the address.

Two Bandits Intercepted Midway Inspector Jin and the patrolmen who were on duty first arrived at the Old Zha Patrol Room and requested assistance. Before they arrived at Room 24, the bandits detected them and fled from the New World. The detectives chased after them and intercepted two robbers on Nanjing Road Yinghua Street and brought them back to the French Patrol Room. After a strict interrogation by the patrol chief, one confessed his name as Zhang Peiqing and the other as Chen Debao, and confessed that the hostage-holding agency was now in a thatched house in Fanjiatun, west of the Hongqiao Airport in western Shanghai. Inspector Jin, after receiving the confession, immediately led the entire team of detectives and patrolmen, all armed and wearing steel armor, and took six cars to Hongqiao.

The search went all the way to Qingpu and arrived at the airport. The Public Security Bureau of the Sixth District, First Precinct, was asked to send police detectives to assist in the arrest. However, the road in the countryside was very narrow and the cars could not pass. The detectives had to get out of the car and walk. Fortunately, the bright moon illuminated the autumn night. The detectives walked more than twenty miles before arriving at Fanjiatun. First, the two bandits identified the location correctly, and the detectives rushed in. However, the bandits had moved to another place the day before. Fortunately, an accomplice was captured in the house, who confessed the location of the new bandit den. The detectives ordered the bandit to lead the way for another ten miles near the border of Qingpu County. They saw a thatched house in the distance and the bandit pointed out that the house was where the hostage was being held. The detectives were preparing to search when the bandits in the house noticed them.

A fierce battle broke out on both sides. When the bandits detected the detectives coming to arrest them, they took out their pistols and opened fire to resist arrest. The detectives also drew their guns and fought back. The two sides fired more than thirty shots in total, lasting about twenty minutes. The bandits were outnumbered and the detectives bravely

stepped forward and captured seven bandits, seizing three pistols with live ammunition.

During the melee, one bandit was shot three times by a detective, wounding his abdomen, leg, right arm. The hostage Xuan Aihou was rescued in the bandit den. At that time, Xuan Jun was startled by the gunshots in the bandit den, and his shock subsided after being rescued. The detectives took the captured bandits, the hostages, and the injured bandits to the airport and returned to the French Patrol Room by car to detain the bandits separately and wait for interrogation and transfer to the government for interrogation.

List of Names of Kidnappers and Hostages Xuan Jun was escorted home, and the injured bandits were sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. The names of the bandits are recorded as follows: Zhang Peiqing, Chen Debao, Zhu Sanni, Zhou Jinsheng, Lu Xiaohai, Chu Yunlong, Xi Xiangsheng, Wang Shuji, Qin Boqiu, Zhang Amao (injured in the hospital), and ten others. By the time the detectives returned to the patrol room after the arrest, the east had broken dawn.

Woman Nearly Suffers Misfortune Due to Placenta Not Removed 142

Zhang Lin Ruifang Accuses Sun Keji

Of Negligence in Stillbirth Surgery

Please Punish for Negligence of Duty

And Pay 5,000 Yuan in Solatium Sun Keji, a doctor hired by the Red Cross Haig Road Hospital, was recently sued by Zhang Lin Ruifang, a woman from Ningbo residing at No. 36 Qinghai Road, by hiring lawyer Ye Shaoying in the Special District Court for negligence of duty causing injury to others. According to her complaint, the plaintiff was 32 years old. She became pregnant in February or March of this year. In July, she was bleeding from her lower body and went to the Red Cross Haig Road General Hospital for treatment. The defendant diagnosed that the fetus had died and needed surgery to make it fall. The plaintiff's husband agreed to be hospitalized. On the 17th, the defendant first anesthetized the plaintiff and then performed the surgery. On the 23rd, the defendant claimed that the plaintiff had recovered and could be discharged from the hospital. The plaintiff paid the hospital ward fee of 60 yuan, the surgery fee of 100 yuan, and the examination fee of 5 yuan, totaling 165 yuan, and had a receipt. After being discharged from the hospital, the abdominal pain was like a streak, and the bleeding was even worse than before the surgery. The plaintiff's husband personally went to the defendant's residence to report and asked him to come home for diagnosis and treatment. Because he refused, he changed to Bao Long Hospital for treatment. After the German doctors Fei Naxu and Mao Deng diagnosed that the previous uterine surgery was negligent and the placenta had not been removed, the condition was very dangerous. The second operation was performed immediately, and the placenta was removed on the spot. According to the German doctor, fortunately, it was discovered early, otherwise, if it was delayed for another day, there would be a risk of life. Based on the above facts, the defendant has obviously constituted the crime in Article 301, Section 2 of the Criminal Law and should be summoned to be punished according to law, and an attached civil suit orders the defendant to pay the plaintiff a solatium of 5,000 yuan. Yesterday, Judge Wu conducted a preliminary hearing and ordered the hearing to be rescheduled.

Grandmother's Redemption of Grandson 144

The efforts of the Child Welfare Association mediated the case of Zhu, an old female servant working at No. 335 Duozhu Mountain Road, Qipu Road, whose two-year-old grandson, Zhu Genfa, was sold by her second son and his wife due to temporary unemployment and difficulty in making ends meet. They sold him for forty yuan to Xie Bingsheng of Lane 1, No. 2, Jiumu Lane, Manzhou Road, as an adopted son. However, the grandmother Zhu was unaware of this sale. After the sale, the old woman was heartbroken, for although she had two sons, this was the only grandson born to her second son. She feared the family line would end and begged Xie to allow her to redeem the child for reunion. However, Xie Bingsheng insisted that the matter was settled by a mutual contract and was privately done, and that he had invited relatives and friends to a banquet to celebrate the adoption. He argued that if he were to allow redemption at will, it would affect his

reputation and insisted on refusing. Xie Bingsheng's old mother, who was about the same age as the old servant Zhu, also deeply loved this adopted grandson and insisted that since he had been bought, he could not be redeemed. Mr. Wei, Zhu's employer, argued with Xie on her behalf, attempting to mediate and offer a monetary redemption, but Xie refused. Seeing the old woman's pain due to his position as her employer, Mr. Wei reported the matter to the China Child Welfare Association. The Association sent Wang Guan'yi and Wang Riru to investigate the circumstances and procedures of the adoption. A Mr. Wang, a relative of Xie Bingsheng, reported on his behalf and verbally promised to return the child upon receiving the money. Zhang, a staff member, photographed the child and registered everything. Afterwards, he went to Qipu Road to inquire about everything from the old servant Zhu, informing her that redemption was possible but required a guarantor. After redeeming the child, he would be sent to be raised by her eldest son in Wuxi to ensure he would not be sold again. A day later, the old servant Zhu provided a written guarantee and asked Mr. Wei Dagang to act as a witness, submitting it to the Child Welfare Association. Wang and Zhang then went to the Xie family

to handle the redemption procedures, with his relative, Mr. Wang, again responsible for the matter. After everything was completed, Zhu was told to prepare the money and paperwork to pick up the child the next day. Unexpectedly, that evening, Mr. Wang and Xie Bingsheng discussed the matter and had a change of heart, insisting on compensation for losses. The Child Welfare Association

had no choice but to let both parties resolve the matter through legal channels. Xie then offered to comply with the Child Welfare Association's proposed solution

and allow Zhu to redeem the child. Therefore, at 3 PM on September 10th, Mr. Wang and Mr. Zhang of the Child Welfare Association, accompanied by Mr. Wei Dagang and old woman Zhu, went to Xie's house, returned the money, prepared gifts, destroyed the contract, burned the receipts, and took Zhu Genfa back. The dispute was finally resolved, and the pearl was returned to its original owner, with the Zhu family reunited.

Child Bride Sent Home 145

Recent Amusing Incident in Wusong

Mother-in-law Casually Asks Date of Birth

Young Bride Confused and Answers Incorrectly

Leading to the Groom's Family Returning the Bride. Mao Asheng, whose ancestral home is Shaoxing, currently resides at the Li family residence in Xizhen, Wusong. He is forty years old, with a gentle, honest, diligent, and thrifty nature. Every day, after finishing his business, he helps his wife with household chores. His wife, Zhao, is about the same age and of medium stature. In her youth, she was beautiful and skilled at handling people, always speaking kindly and pleasantly, so everyone nearby knew of her as "Mother Asheng." They have two sons, the eldest named Mao Xi, who is fifteen years old. Zhao is planning to find a child bride to avoid difficulties in finding a suitable marriage later.

Encountering Baozhen as a Daughter-in-Law. Zhou Jiaqi, who lives nearby, has a relative named Gong, a widow from Beixin Town, Chongming. Her family is poor, and she has six children, half boys and half girls. Since her husband died, she has no support. This spring, she brought her daughter Baozhen, who is thirteen years old, strong, and pretty, to Wusong to stay at Zhou's house, seeking a spouse. Zhao learned of this and, upon seeing the girl, found her perfect. As the opportunity arose, she feared losing the chance and asked Zhou to act as matchmaker. They agreed on a betrothal gift of eighty-four yuan, and the girl was immediately betrothed and began living with the Mao family as a child bride. After Baozhen came to the family, she ate and went everywhere with Mao Xi. Asheng and his wife were delighted to see the young couple getting along so well, and their family life was happy. Who would have thought that troubles would arise, which were beyond anticipation?

Suddenly Asking the Date of Birth. One day, Zhao had nothing to do and suddenly asked Baozhen when her birthday was. Although the girl was tall, her mind was still immature. Suddenly asked by her mother-in-law, she panicked and answered incorrectly. Zhao became suspicious and unhappy. Busy-bodies further speculated that the girl was a widow, etc. Zhao ignored what others said but was more anxious after hearing this. Fearing that keeping the girl would be detrimental to her son, she discussed returning her to her mother's home with her husband. Asheng did not agree because there was no evidence. Zhao argued with her husband every day, and the sound of quarreling never ceased. She even cried every day. Asheng was by nature gentle and tolerant and used those words to deal with his wife, but Zhao only became more suspicious.

Abandoning Husband and Son to Flee. One day, Zhao took advantage of her husband's absence on business and fled alone with a small bundle. When Asheng returned home and found out, he searched everywhere but found no trace. It was not until two weeks later that he learned Zhao had returned to her mother's home in Shaoxing. He went to welcome her back, but she seemed to have mental problems. Later, neighbors advised Asheng that if he did not divorce the girl, the old couple might not be able to protect themselves fully. Therefore, Asheng agreed.

Unmarried Couple Separated. After Asheng discussed and finalized the matter with the matchmaker the other day, he notified Baozhen's mother, Gong. Gong immediately returned to Wusong and refunded all the betrothal money. Asheng also returned the horoscopes, and the girl was taken away by her mother. From then on,

they parted ways, and the couple became strangers.

Hereby, citizens of this city, Zhang Qiutang, Lin Zhizhong, and Wang Youzhai, have sent a letter to various agencies requesting a strict prohibition of red pills to eliminate the scourge of drugs. The letter states (details omitted): In our humble opinion, the harm of red pills is greater than that of opium. Those in the lower classes who cannot afford to smoke opium often use red pills as a substitute. As a result, the sales of red pills have increased, and the harm caused by red pills has deepened. Although the authorities have repeatedly issued strict prohibitions, these have had little effect within the concessions, where prohibitions are lax, and sellers and users are everywhere. It is even heard that those involved in this trade have large-scale organizations, with some people responsible for transporting the pills and others for selling them. Some are even blatant and never exposed. For example, Yao Guiji and others in the French Concession sell as much as several million yuan worth of red pills annually. According to a report on the sixth (of this month), the police arrested a woman selling red pills at No. 790 Fujian Road. Although the court sentenced her to imprisonment and a fine, the source of the red pills was not thoroughly investigated, and the cunning merchants who package and transport the pills can still evade the law. To expect the elimination of drugs in such a way is like climbing a tree to catch fish. If this situation is not remedied, our people will ultimately perish from red pills even if they do not die from opium. Qiutang and others, witnessing this, feel heartbroken and cannot remain silent. Therefore, they jointly appeal to you to quickly urge the concession authorities to strictly prohibit red pills and show no leniency, so that the cunning merchants who sell drugs can be brought to justice and the people’s anger can be appeased, and the scourge of drugs can be eliminated. Soldier Zhou Han Wounded Last night around 7 p.m., Zhou Han, a soldier from Jiangxi stationed in the First Battalion, Twenty-Sixth Regiment, Thirteenth Brigade, Fifth Division of the South City, was traveling on the Hua Shang Route 3 circular tram No. 45 from Laoximen on business. (7) A proposal to improve postal services and prioritize the development of postal affairs in the future was approved and entrusted to the eighth executive and supervisory committee to plan and implement. (8) Temporary motions: 1. Representative Wu Yaxiong of the eighth branch proposed that the union's seventh committee worked hard and achieved remarkable results. The various branches and special groups should purchase gifts separately to commemorate the union. The motion was passed, and the representatives of the various branches and special groups were responsible for handling it. 2. Representative Cheng Zuoqing of the tenth branch proposed that the union should provide separate pensions to members who retire due to old age, are incapacitated due to illness, or are injured on duty, and that the union's pension regulations should be revised to benefit the sick and weak. The motion was passed and referred to the eighth executive committee for handling. 3. A motion to limit the passing score for all levels of qualification examinations to 60 points was referred to the eighth executive committee for discussion. 4. A motion regarding branch offices was referred to the eighth committee for discussion.

The meeting adjourned at 7 o'clock.

The French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union convened an emergency meeting yesterday to discuss and resolve the following: (1) Zhou Da, a worker in the railway department, was fired by the foreman for fighting. All the workers in the department demanded that the foreman reinstate the fired worker. The union convened the foreman, Xiao Lazi, to discuss the matter. As Zhou Da could not be reinstated by the company, it was resolved that the foreman Xiao Lazi would provide Zhou Da with 10 yuan per month, and someone would be responsible for guaranteeing it. (2) Li Linshu of the Transportation Department colluded with the capitalists to oppress workers, forcibly collect membership dues, and secretly organize a workers' club to disrupt the union's proceedings. How should this be handled? It was resolved to petition the higher authorities to strictly investigate and punish him.

The preparatory committee of the joint association of the Shanghai Cigarette, Publishing, Machinery, Shipbuilding, Silk, Yarn, Water and Electricity Workers' Unions hereby notifies all workers in the city in the aforementioned industries that the registration of the various industry unions has begun. The original text is recorded as follows: Notification. This association is entrusted by the Municipal Party Department to prepare for the joint association of various industries. The work has already begun. It is hoped that the various industry unions will come to the association for registration starting from today and submit the registration forms separately. This matter concerns the interests of the various industry unions themselves. Do not delay. This is hereby notified. September 13, 1930, Republic of China. Education News Highlights

The Su-Yi Educational Office Investigates Local Education 156

The Jiangsu Province Preparatory Office for Compulsory Education, in order to conduct a practical investigation of local education, has hired Jin Yingyuan as an investigator and correspondence course student itinerant instructor. A special letter was sent to the education bureaus of various counties, stating: "As the period of political tutelage begins, many things need to be done. The vigorous implementation of universal education is particularly urgent. Since the establishment of our office, we have been actively studying the issue of universal education with the cooperation and assistance of the education bureaus of various counties. We have never ceased our efforts. We have long recognized the importance of issues such as teacher training and education statistics, and have been praised by the central and provincial education administrative agencies. However, considering the vast area of our province, further concrete research on the special needs of various counties cannot be achieved merely through circular surveys and discussions. Moreover, our office, on behalf of teacher training, has nearly 2,000 correspondence course students who have spread across more than 50 counties. We should also send personnel to guide them from time to time to increase actual education efficiency. Now, we have specially hired Mr. Jin Yingyuan as the local education investigator and correspondence course student itinerant instructor to actively work in various counties. Mr. Jin has served as a special commissioner for local education in Jiangsu Province, as well as teaching positions in provincial and county normal schools and experimental primary schools, and as the director of the county education bureau. He has sufficient knowledge and experience. In the future, his achievements should be considerable. When he arrives in your county, we hope you will provide him with assistance, allow him to stay, and provide him with food and transportation at his own expense. In addition to separate letters, we are sending this letter to inform you. Please investigate and act accordingly."

Sports

Shanghai Westerners' Football Association Annual Meeting Resolutions 164

Elected New Officers, Amended Article 41 of the Bylaws, Restricting Teams Added to Eight From Competing Outside the City. The Official Season is Scheduled to Begin on October 11, and Friendly Matches Will Begin on October 4th. The Shanghai Westerners' Football Association held its annual meeting at the Asia Literary Society the day before yesterday. Vice President Ford chaired the meeting. After passing the annual work report and financial statements, the new officers were elected. Grimshaw was elected as the President, Ford, Quail, and Leder as Vice Presidents, Hamson as the Secretary, and White Ting as the Secretary and Referee Chairman. Stethard, Edward, and Peterkiss were elected as committee members, all of whom were re-elected. Then, it was proposed to amend the bylaws by deleting the words "or the Chinese Physical Education Advancement Association" listed in parentheses in Article 41, making the bracketed text the main text of the article, and deleting the small note attached to the parentheses for explanation. After some discussion by Belachan, Hamson, and Peterkiss, and a substantial explanation by Hao Boyang of the General Association, it was passed by the members. According to Article 41 of the bylaws, in general, any club, team, or member of a team that joins the Westerners' Football Association may not go to another city to play a game or participate in a game not organized by the association (Chinese Physical Education Advancement Association) without the prior consent of the association's executive committee. The executive committee has the right to review all financial accounts for going to another city to play a game. The words "or the Chinese Physical Education Advancement Association" were initially added by resolution of the executive committee without being passed by the general meeting, so a bracket was added with a small note explaining the origin. Now it is proposed to ratify this at the general meeting, hence this proposal to amend the bylaws. Furthermore, the association has scheduled the official season to begin on October 11, and friendly matches will begin on October 4.

郵務乒乓隊大勝日本隊 166

Postal Ping Pong Team Triumphs Over Japanese Team

Last night, the postal ping pong team competed against the visiting Shanghai-based Japanese ping pong team at the Postal Association on Xingjia Road. Over three hundred spectators were present, with latecomers unable to find standing room. At eight o'clock, referees Yu Binqi and Ikeda commenced the match. After three hours of intense competition, the postal team emerged victorious with an 8-1 win. During the match, the Japanese team's advantage lay with Tsuda, whose defensive skills were excellent. The postal team's Zhu Fanglin performed exceptionally well. In the final match, Sengoku faced Li Chuanshu. Sengoku, a strong player for the Japanese team, met his match in Li. The contest was intense, with both players demonstrating excellent attacking and defending skills. However, Li's experience proved decisive, securing a 3-0 victory. It was suggested that against another opponent, victory might have been harder to attain. After the match, the team captain, Xu Wu, hosted a tea and refreshments reception for all match officials. Following a short speech, a one-meter long-distance running champion, Chen Xuzhou, provided interpretation. The event concluded around midnight.

中華遠征足球隊勝棉蘭中華 167

Chinese Expedition Football Team Defeats Medan Chinese Team

3-2, Winning with a Penalty Kick

(August 28, Medan Correspondence) The Chinese Expedition Football Team arrived in Medan from Singapore on August 26th, scheduled to play four matches. The first match was against the Medan Chinese Football Team on the 27th, the second against the East Sumatra Football Team on the 29th, the third against the Dutch United Team on September 1st, and the fourth against the Asian United Team on September 2nd. Among these four teams, the East Sumatra United Team is considered the strongest, while the Chinese team is the weakest. The Asian team is also not to be underestimated. The following is a record of the first match.

The match between the Expedition Team and the Chinese team was the former's debut in Medan. Overall, the Expedition Team won effortlessly, seemingly without fully displaying their skills. The Chinese team, while putting in a strenuous effort, also showed moments of brilliance and should not be dismissed. The final score was 3-2 in favor of the Expedition Team, as detailed below:

球塲觀衆人山人海 168

Stadium Crowded with Spectators

Although the Expedition Team was not evenly matched with their opponent, many people came to watch their debut. The match was scheduled for 5:00 PM, but as early as 3:00 PM, people were already searching for seats. As the time approached, the stadium was packed with spectators. Ticket scalpers inflated the price from seven to eight or nine *fang* [currency unit], forcing those eager to enter to pay an extra one or two *fang*.

（二）領事開球健兒奔逐 169

(2) Consul Kicks Off, Players Dash

Before the match, the Expedition Team practiced, drawing applause and cheers for their impressive moves. At 4:45 PM, the Expedition Team took a photo, followed by the Chinese team. After the coin toss to decide the kick-off and field selection, the two teams posed for a group photo. Then, Mr. Zuo Lin Shen, the Chinese Consul in Medan, kicked off the match. As the whistle blew, the players from both sides dashed onto the field. In the initial stages, the Expedition Team seemed in no hurry to attack, focusing on passing the ball while showcasing individual skills. The Chinese team played cautiously and diligently, managing to penetrate the Expedition Team's defense several times.

（三）中華獲球放砲慶祝 170

(3) Chinese Team Scores, Celebrations Erupt

At 5:15 PM, two Chinese forwards charged towards the goal. Zhou Xianyan, the goalkeeper, rushed to defend, but was overwhelmed by the attack. The ball was cleared but fell to the Chinese midfielder, who slotted it into the net. Zhou, already out of position, was unable to save the shot. The Chinese team scored the first goal, triggering celebratory firecrackers.

（四）球怪舉足人人狂呼 171

(4) A Peculiar Kick, Everyone Cheers Wildly

The Expedition Team remained unfazed by the goal and continued to play without urgency. At 5:25 PM, the Chinese goal was under siege. Dai Linjing, Chen Yutian, and Chen Guangyao all had powerful shots, but the Chinese goalkeeper made excellent saves. At 5:26 PM, Li Huitang battled with two Chinese defenders for the ball. Li flicked the ball backwards with his foot, gaining possession and shooting from the spot. The shot was not particularly fast, but it was perfectly placed, curving towards the right corner of the goal. The goalkeeper was caught off guard, and the ball sailed into the net. Spectators gasped at the brilliance of the play. After leveling the score, the Expedition Team gradually displayed their skills, putting the Chinese team on the defensive. The Expedition Team launched frequent attacks, and had the Chinese goalkeeper been less capable, the score could have been much higher.

五遠射高擊隨心所欲 172

(5) Long Shot, High Strike, As You Wish

At 5:35 PM, Li Huitang took a long-range shot. The ball flew high, hit the top of the goalpost, bounced down, and landed directly into the net. The goalkeeper was unable to react. The Expedition Team scored, taking a 2-1 lead. The Expedition Team continued their attack until halftime. The first half ended with the Expedition Team winning 2-1. In the second half, play alternated between the two teams. A Chinese defender committed a foul, resulting in a free kick. Li Huitang took the kick, and the ball flew into the net. The Expedition Team scored their third goal. From then on, the Expedition Team focused on displaying their skills rather than attacking, even when they reached the Chinese goal.

（六）中華健兒最後奮鬥 173

(6) Chinese Players' Last-Ditch Effort

Unexpectedly, as the match neared its end, the Chinese players launched a fierce counterattack. At 6:00 PM, the Chinese forward passed the ball past the Expedition Team's final line of defense. The right winger crossed the ball to the center, approaching the Expedition Team's goal. Zhou Xianyan rushed out to intercept, but was unable to prevent a goal. The second half ended with a 1-1 draw, resulting in an overall score of 3-2 in favor of the Expedition Team, with one penalty kick.

（七）綜觀球藝責備賢者 174

(7) Overview of Skills, Criticizing the Talented

In terms of individual skills, the Expedition Team's players were impeccable. However, their performance was overly playful, leading to a less than satisfactory result. Those unfamiliar with the Expedition Team might say that only Li Huitang stood out, while the others were mediocre. This is perhaps a misconception, as teamwork and individual effort were not fully displayed. Some argue that the Chinese team was not a worthy opponent for the Expedition Team, limiting their performance. Perhaps this is true, but the match on September 1st against a stronger opponent will reveal the Expedition Team's true potential. (It is reported that on the 1st, the Expedition Team will face the Dutch United Team, with the Dutch Royal Family Celebration Committee donating a silver cup to the winner.)

自由談 180

Free Talk

付之一笑 181

Laugh It Off

— Hai Ke

Wife A: How are things going at the girls' vocational school you run?

Wife B: Couldn't be better! No one can compare to me.

Wife A: Really? So your students have great career prospects after graduation?

Wife B: Of course! They not only gain a profession, but also end up marrying their employers, becoming the boss's wife or the Prime Minister's wife!

Son: Mother, was Adam the ancestor of all people?

Mother: Yes, he was the first person in the world.

Son: So he didn't have a father?

Mother: Of course not.

Son: How lucky he was!

Tourist A: Yesterday, I overheard a story from the sedan chair carriers.

Tourist B: What happened?

Tourist A: The day before yesterday, in the evening, they saw a young gentleman and a beautiful lady walking up the mountain together. They walked higher and higher, and then they didn't see them come back.

Tourist B: How terrible, something must have happened to them.

Tourist A: Wait, they went down on the other side of the mountain.

Wife (walking into the bedroom and seeing a thief opening a drawer): Hey! What are you doing here?

Thief (in a respectful tone): Following the missus's orders. Whatever you want me to do, I'll do it.

總理首次起義紀念瑣聞 182

Anecdotes from the Commemoration of the Premier's First Uprising

— Sun Choucheng

This newspaper has already reported on the commemoration of the Premier's first uprising, held by various sectors of the city at the Fangbang Bridge Republican Cinema. Here are some trivial details I observed that day. I arrived at the venue at 9:00 AM. The entrance was packed with people. Fortunately, there were Boy Scouts standing on both sides to maintain order, allowing me to push through the crowd, sign my name, and receive a printed leaflet from the propaganda department. Upon examining it, it detailed the events of the Premier's uprising in Guangzhou eighteen years before the founding of the Republic. At that time, after the Sino-Japanese War, the navy was destroyed, and the country's defense was lost. Taking advantage of the public's anger, the Premier and Lu Haodong secretly went to Guangzhou to start an uprising. After taking my seat, I observed that about 70% of the representatives present were under the age of thirty, and the remaining 30% were under the age of forty. I jokingly said to a friend next to me, "When the Premier launched his first uprising, most of the representatives from various groups attending today were not even born yet. Now they are all followers of the Premier, which demonstrates the effectiveness of the Three Principles of the People being believed by everyone." Hanging on the stage was an enamel bust of the Premier. The four walls were covered with various slogans written on three-foot-wide and four-foot-long white paper, such as "(Commemorate September 9th, expedite unification, develop production, and solve people's livelihood problems)" and "(Commemorate September 9th, abide by the Premier's instructions)," which were very eye-catching. Yang Qingyuan, the Minister of Propaganda, presided over the meeting and reported the purpose of the meeting. He detailed the Premier's various revolutionary experiences and difficulties from the first uprising in Guangzhou at the age of 36 to the opposition to Yuan Shikai. He also mentioned that some comrades within the party felt that the revolutionary spirit was generally declining, and that they should invigorate their spirits, continue the Premier's legacy from the first uprising, and strive forward until the Premier's instructions were fully realized. When Tong Xingbai spoke, he recounted the Premier's original intention of the uprising, the reasons for its failure, and the Premier's continued and tireless efforts after the failure. He presented the information as if counting family treasures, making it a history of the revolution. His composed demeanor and accurate statements earned him a lot of applause. The weather was unusually hot that day. The venue was crowded, making the temperature very high. Some people who did not bring folding fans used their hats and the printed leaflets from the propaganda department as fans, waving them non-stop. From a distance, they looked like butterflies fluttering in the wind, which was quite a sight. Most of the female comrades were sweating profusely, wiping their faces with handkerchiefs. The sound of complaining about the heat was endless. A certain school led more than a hundred students to participate in the meeting. Because there were no seats in front of the stage, they went upstairs. The crowd was noisy, causing the speaker to stop speaking for three minutes due to the overpowering sound. The Boy Scouts from the labor union training institute worked hard to maintain order, and the meeting was finally restored. The main points of the other speeches were: commemoration should not focus on formalities but on practical action, and revolution requires first reforming the heart in order to be just and selfless. I returned home and recorded this to remember and not forget.

臭鄰 183

Stinky Neighbor

— Fei Jiaobao

Accountant Tai Baosun told me a rather strange story yesterday. His office has always been next to a toilet. When he first joined the accounting department of the Commodity Exchange, there was a toilet next door. Later, when he joined the accounting department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company as an assistant, the office next door was also a toilet. He thought it was a coincidence at first, but recently, when he joined the Sanbei Steamship Company, his office was in a corner of a small building with a rather quiet environment. He opened a small door in his office and was shocked to see another toilet. He wondered why this was the case and why he was so destined to be near toilets. Someone said that these "yellow and white objects" [money] contain a lot of ammonia. Since Mr. Xiong's job is to be with money day and night, the ammonia can be used to awaken his spirit when he is surrounded by the stench of money. Is this the reason? (Returned Payment)

客述曾農髯之度量 184

A Guest Recounts Zeng Nongran's Magnanimity

— Kengbo

Zeng Nongran of Hengyang is a well-known calligrapher in Shanghai. Nowadays, a bad habit has emerged: whenever a calligrapher or painter becomes famous, their works are often imitated. Often, counterfeit products flood the market, and the skillful imitators can even deceive the eye. A guest recounted that one day Zeng Nongran was chatting at a friend's house when a housemate brought four short screens and asked the friend to identify whether they were genuine or fake Zeng's works. As soon as the friend saw them, he knew they were fake, so he smiled and said to the housemate, "This gentleman is Zeng Nongran himself. You can ask him to look at them." Zeng glanced at them and nodded, saying, "These are indeed my writings. There is nothing wrong with them." The friend remained silent. The housemate was overjoyed and said, "Everyone said they were fake because the price was too low, but now that Mr. Zeng says there is nothing wrong with them, all my doubts are dispelled." After the housemate left, the friend said, "Aren't you worried about damaging your reputation by casually admitting that they are genuine?" Zeng smiled and said, "Calligraphy and painting are mere objects. What harm is there if fake ones can deceive the eye? Those who rely on imitating my name for a living would starve to death on the costly Shanghai sea if no one recklessly collected them. I can't help people in need. Why be stingy with this small indirect benefit and argue with them? How petty would that be!" The friend praised him, saying, "You are truly a generous man, beyond our reach." Another person recounted that a fellow villager of Zeng showed Zeng a scroll with Zeng's signature, which was also a counterfeit. Zeng saw that the writing was too poor, so he falsely said, "I wrote this after I recovered from a sickness." He then took a brush and added two lines in a blank space, saying, "I wrote this in the past, when I had just recovered from my illness. My wrist strength was completely gone. Looking at it again today, I am filled with shame. Therefore, I write these few words to show my fault." Those who saw it said that these thirty words were extremely lively and wonderful. From the above, it can be seen that Zeng's magnanimity is remarkable. Mencius said, "Those who hear of the ways of Liu Xiahui become generous. The stingy become generous." The same can be said of Mr. Zeng.

電影進步譚 185

A Discussion on the Progress of Film

— Miao Xiu

When Theda Bara rewatches the short comic films she assisted Roscoe Arbuckle in making, or when Rowland V. Lee rewatches the moustache detective films he made before, and then you teach them to watch their newly successful talkie, they are probably getting some sense of old and new. Within these sentiments are several ingredients: A kind of technological progress, a kind of shifting direction, a kind of career success, and a kind of hope to improve further.

Let's think about it. How many years of history does foreign film have? It is not easy to have today's achievements in natural evolution and the efforts of participating molecules. Recalling our China, in this industrially backward and unstable society, all construction has little progress, but the film industry can still struggle under this environment. Although it is not as good as the United States, this spirit is also worth our reflection.

Therefore, those who expect the progress of our country's film industry should not say how good foreign films are and how inferior our country's films are, because history is not as long as theirs, capital is not as sufficient as theirs, the environment is not as stable as theirs, and the audience is not as universal as theirs. Naturally, our country's films should be backward. But in fact, if we can really make a scientific comparison of history, capital, etc., I am afraid that today's Chinese films are not as far behind foreign films as they were yesterday. It is only strange that a generation of people think that foreign films are always good, while Chinese films are not worth a glance. This kind of foreign-flattering mentality is enough to destroy the country. If I tell them the fact that the Japanese love their own films and reject American films, I am afraid it is no less than writing a small history of national humiliation.

Recently I have seen two good films, such as the Star Film Company's "A Romantic Woman" (Chinese film) and the Fox Company's "Sunny Side Up" (foreign film). Although I dare not say that "A Romantic Woman" is better than "Sunny Side Up", in fact, why must it be said that Miss Xuan Jinglin's performance is not as good as Janet Gaynor's?

Ah, what is lacking is that Chinese films are silent films, while foreign films are all talkies. Then here I hope that the Star Film Company's "Sing-Song Girl Red Peony" will be released quickly so that ordinary Chinese people who follow the trend can also see Chinese films with complete dialogue and can understand that there are indeed people in domestic films who are working hard and moving towards the road to success.

南洋游記（四七） 186

Travels in Southeast Asia (47)

— Linghua

On the ship, I met a Malay merchant who was a Christian and could speak English. I talked to him about the true meaning of Jesus, who did not spread his teachings with cannons but offered the right cheek after being struck on the left. I compared this with the different approaches of Eastern cultures like Confucianism and Buddhism, which are more powerful than today's Westernization. The Malay man said that India is now in revolution, and Gandhi has been arrested, indicating a resurgence of Eastern nations. I said that it is not only the use of force by nations that matters, but also Eastern culture should use moral education to save the West. He agreed to promote my Kunhua Datong Doctrine [a doctrine of universal harmony and equality].

Life on the ship is very good for health, so Westerners often use sea voyages as a way to recover from illness. Why don't Chinese people learn from this? Every time I travel by ship, I feel it is much better than being on land. The environment is quiet, and worries are far away. Reading, writing poetry, and enjoying the sea clouds are very pleasant.

Since the death of my mother, I studied Buddhism under Mr. Gui Bohua in Japan for fourteen years and became accustomed to abstaining from meat and fish. In recent years, I have often traveled to Guangdong and Guangxi and sometimes have been involved in military affairs. In places where the water and soil are not suitable, and food is inconvenient, I have great difficulty. I feel uncomfortable even if I eat a little fish or shrimp. But on the Western ship, eating Western food, under the influence of the environment, I also eat beef. The smell of fish and meat is just as Yuan Zicai described: "I hold my nose and swallow quickly, unable to distinguish the taste." But recently, I obtained a Collection of Protecting Life Paintings, which uses Buddhist compassion to create paintings, and my friend Ma Yifu wrote a preface, quoting the poems of Su Shi and Bai Juyi about eating vegetarian food, describing opening a can as opening a coffin. After reading it, my old ideas resurfaced, and I can no longer hold my nose and swallow fishy things. The power of psychology is so great.

On the 11th, at 7:00 AM, we arrived at Port Klang and stopped until 5:00 PM. I disembarked with Mr. Chen and took a car to the Guanyin Temple, costing only 30 cents per person because we shared a ride. The Guanyin Temple is a small temple, but the temples in Southeast Asia are all very beautiful and clean. This is probably just the original name, which has been used until now, and it is no longer just a pavilion. Mr. Zhuang Mingchuan was very welcoming. There were many women offering incense. Unfortunately, they were all illiterate. The rickshaws here are wider than in Singapore. At 9:00 AM, we took a car to Kuala Lumpur, costing 1.60 yuan for both of us. We allowed it to pick up passengers along the way. We passed several large iron bridges and small river bridges. The forest was deep and quiet. The workers were in the rubber forest, and the weather was not hot. The rubber forest was very clean. Sometimes, red houses could be seen nestled in the forest, which were the villages of the local people. My friend Lin Fuyan from Java has repeatedly told me, "If you travel to Java, you can prove Lao Tzu's ancient Datong philosophy, and you will realize that Confucius's teachings are inferior to Lao Tzu's, and that Lao Tzu's teachings can truly achieve great governance." I believe him. Now, although I have only briefly arrived in Kuala Lumpur and passed through the countryside, I already feel that I can prove most of it without having to go to Java.

Heart's Warmth (275) 187

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo's Tears Stain a Maiden's Heart, Red Lotus Sheds, a Young Woman's Soul Departs

Who knew that less than three months after Cuiyun's marriage, the situation would change drastically, and even Zhang Yiqing's attitude would change? This was like the rulers of dynasties who, upon seizing power, spoke of eliminating tyranny and bringing peace, reducing punishments and lessening taxes, but once they had gained power, they revealed their autocratic faces and used all sorts of means to oppress you. Cuiyun inquired and found out that he had a wife living in the countryside of Ningbo who didn't come to Shanghai. This was true. He returned to Ningbo once a year, or sometimes once every two or three years. This was also true. His wife was a country woman from Ningbo, very ugly and clumsy, like a rough servant. Zhang Yiqing didn't like her; this was even more true. But in addition to this, there was another woman. Zhang Yiqing hadn't told his friends, and he wasn't willing to reveal her. Unexpectedly, Cuiyun didn't know that this old woman left in the countryside of Ningbo was Zhang Yiqing's original wife, his wife from his humble beginnings. This was the woman his parents had found for him when he was an apprentice in a small shop, and of course, she didn't suit his taste. When he became successful, he secretly took a lover in Shanghai. This woman was said to be the wife of one of his friends, also a fellow native of Ningbo. This fellow townsman was ten years older than Zhang Yiqing. He had worked hard all his life and just managed to accumulate seventy or eighty thousand in assets, but as soon as he had wealth, his health failed. It was truly (After gathering nectar from a hundred flowers to make honey, for whom is he busy?). He died of consumption, leaving behind a young widow. This was originally a second wife, nineteen years younger than her husband. This fellow townsman was a good friend of Zhang Yiqing. On his deathbed, he entrusted this young widow to Zhang Yiqing, asking him to take care of everything. Who knew (entrusting a chick to a weasel)? Zhang Yiqing didn't care about the friendship with the deceased. He used his means to seize her, like Zhong Jinshi collecting gifts. He took everything, people and belongings, without exception. Emperor Zhaolie entrusted his son to Zhuge Kongming, saying, "If he can be assisted, then assist him. If he cannot be assisted, then take over yourself." Now Zhang Yiqing had only added half a character to Liu Xuande's edict of entrusting the orphan, turning it into "If she can be assisted, then assist her. If she cannot be assisted, then marry her." He also did his utmost for his old friend's widow. Originally, the old friend's wife had been married to her husband for less than five years before becoming a widow. Her youth was cut short like this, and she had no children. Zhang Yiqing, bearing the weight of the entrusted orphan, often came to inquire. He had abandoned his poor wife in the countryside, and he himself was like a single man. A lonely man and a lonely woman are like dry wood and a raging fire. This was only natural. Moreover, Zhang Yiqing's skills were originally good, so not even three full years after his old friend's death, he had already taken his place.

The political turmoil in Japan has had a major impact. Yesterday, the 12th, the official gold price suddenly plummeted, with drastic changes. It is believed that the turmoil in the Japanese cabinet has raised concerns about a potential devaluation, affecting exchange rates. Bills of exchange have also loosened, causing great panic and anxiety. There was an oversupply in the market. Companies such as Yuan Mao, Yongfu Chang, Yongcheng Chang, etc., rushed to sell. Copper Coin Market Rises Steadily 191

This is a natural phenomenon. The same applies to the sluggishness of the currency system. Therefore, although the market price of copper coins has not risen dramatically, its steady upward trend has been clearly visible to us. The underlying reason is that the mint's exports have decreased while demand remains constant, leading to an imbalance between supply and demand. Yarn and Cotton Market Decline Not Weak 193

The yarn market is indeed affected by the global situation, so it is difficult to support the building alone.

Near-term domestic marks and foreign marks both fell. At the opening of the domestic mark market, prices for American cotton turned down, and retail investors sold unanimously. The market sentiment was particularly loose, and prices fell steadily. Each month fell by 9 cents to 1 tael 12 cents. In the afternoon, many bulls cut their positions, and each month fell by another 2, 3, 4, 5, and 6 cents. The total transaction volume for the day was 25,050 bales. Cotton Market Moves to a Soft Territory 194

Daily changes were very fast, making it difficult to grasp. Hengde Hao purchased about 20,000 to 30,000 dan on behalf of Wuxi merchants, but Rui Da sold 20,000 dan. The cotton market is still pessimistic in terms of its actual position. Because various factories have purchased enough Indian cotton, Chinese and foreign yarn factories have no activity. It is said that 24 Indian cotton yarn factories have stopped work, and there is a surplus of raw materials, so there may be changes in the future. Grain River Below Rice Market Firm and Weak Mixed 196

North Gate: Yesterday, fewer than ten rice boats were seen on the river below, and trucks arrived continuously. Sales in the market were still good. Due to the sunny weather, people in the North Gang were slightly less enthusiastic about the broken japonica rice, and the market situation was slightly weaker. High-quality goods were still valued at zero yuan six jiao, and top-quality goods were rare, at around zero yuan eight jiao. Although medium-grade goods were not thick, the price was slightly lower. New japonica rice from Xixin was not seen yet, but it was heard that two or three boats would arrive in the market today. The source of new japonica rice from Dongxin was very scarce. Most industries were hoarding and selling at a premium, so the price soared by half a yuan to one yuan, reaching as high as eighteen yuan and a half to eighteen yuan. New Yangjian shipments were slightly soft by more than two jiao. Ordinary goods opened at fifteen yuan, but the morning market traded at fifteen yuan two jiao, then immediately fell back. The situation was ordinary. New Kejian's arrival was very lively, but sales in the market were slightly sluggish due to the sunny weather, and the price opened at fourteen yuan, which was one or two jiao lower than the previous day. Bai Yuan's arrival and sales were evenly matched, and the market situation was similar to the previous day. High-quality goods were priced at eighteen yuan eight jiao.

South Shanghai: The river arrivals were sparse, and sales on this street were particularly active. Unfortunately, the inventory of each type of goods was exhausted. Therefore, after the drastic increase in the price of white broken japonica rice from the Su-Tong gang, it failed to fall yesterday. High-quality goods were still around twenty yuan, and Zhongguan barely opened at nineteen yuan five or six jiao. The situation was no less than the previous day. For now, it is temporarily stable. Fortunately, there are no Chang gang goods arriving here. The source of thin early rice from the South Gang was also scarce, with high-quality goods at twenty yuan eight jiao. Purchasing activity was normal. The goods arriving in Shanghai from New Yangjian were not very prosperous, and sales were slightly weak. High-quality goods here were around fourteen yuan and a half.

More Customer Xian Rice Arrives, Prices Rise 197

Yesterday, the arrival of various early season rices, especially foreign rice, was floating in the market, and early inventories had been sold out. The remaining hoarded goods and a small number of unsold rice were not easily sold, so the market turned stiff. The price of Zhongguan goods from Jiangxi Ji Zaosheng rose by nearly a jiao again. However, the customer gangs were all watching, and only this street was buying. The number of transactions was actually less than the previous day. A total of 700 bags of Jiangxi Ji Zao Sheng were sold at a price of twelve yuan nine jiao to twelve yuan eight jiao, 300 bags of Hunan rice were sold at a price of eleven yuan nine jiao, and 200 bags of Jiangxi Zao Cao Mi were sold at a price of ten yuan zero nine jiao. The remaining arrivals and sales were lacking.

Afternoon Flour Market Slumps 198

Lifting of Ban Dulls Market; Factories Place Orders. Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the prices of various months showed signs of firming up. This was due to rumors that Tianjin was in urgent need of military supplies and was relying heavily on Shanghai flour for support. Shanghai factories, for various reasons, were also hoping that the ban on flour transport would be lifted soon. It was believed that the ban would be lifted in a few days, which led to expectations of increased demand and higher prices, hence the slight upward trend in the morning. However, by the afternoon,

the possibility of lifting the ban became uncertain again. Furthermore, there were rumors that factories had already placed orders for foreign wheat at around 5 taels per Shanghai tael. As a result, the market not only failed to rise but also declined, with prices for various months trending downward. Although the Tianjin route has been opened, the market may see a temporary rebound, but in reality, this will mainly benefit the factories' production. The settlement prices for this month remained unchanged, October decreased by 0.005 taels, November decreased by 0.0125 taels, December and January decreased by 0.0075 taels, and February decreased by 0.005 taels.

Distant Futures Wheat Market Weakens 199

Yesterday, in the futures wheat market, prices for various months showed a trend of near-term weakness and distant-term strength in both the morning and afternoon trading sessions. The current month's price increased due to some short covering, which boosted market sentiment. Distant months' prices, however, weakened due to foreign wheat quotes being lower by 0.2, 0.3, or 0.4 taels, and also because factories had already started placing orders for foreign wheat at favorable prices, with the option to choose better quality goods. Yesterday, a telegraph from a foreign firm quoted No. 2 wheat at around 5 taels per Shanghai tael, leading to further orders. As a result, distant months' prices weakened again. The settlement price for the current month was 0.04 taels higher than the previous day, October was 0.01 taels higher, November was 0.01 taels lower, December was 0.02 taels lower, January was 0.04 taels lower, and February was 0.02 taels lower. The spot wheat market remained sluggish, with factories showing no inclination to aggressively increase purchases. Opening prices were 0.01 or 0.02 taels lower. Over 2,000 bags of wheat from Shandong, Haizhou, and Haimen were offered, with Shen Da buying over 1,000 bags, and the rest remaining unassigned.

Sugar Market: Domestic Sugar Suddenly Rises 200

Yesterday, sugar market reports from producing areas indicated that the current price of Cuban raw sugar remained at 1.125, and the New York futures price for September was 1.08, unchanged from the previous report. The December price was 1.16, and the March price next year was 1.285, with May at 1.37, each rising by 0.01. The current price of Java raw sugar remained at 0.875, and the futures price for September was 0.850, February was 0.825, and November was 0.8125, each decreasing by 0.0125 to 0.025. At the local Chamber of Commerce market, the buying interest in Dutch No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar remained weak. The asking price was 8 taels, but buyers were only willing to pay 7.9 taels. Sellers were unwilling to sell at a loss, leading to a stalemate and a dull market atmosphere with no transactions. Finely ground white sugar was priced at 8.12 taels, and No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was priced at 7.65 taels, with trading also sluggish. There was even less interest in Dutch brown sugar. Domestic sugar saw a slight increase in price due to the temporary improvement in sentiment after the Minghua factory stopped production and demand showed a slight increase. The transaction price for "Mack" brand was 8.125 taels, "ET" brand was 8.1 taels, "ER" brand was 8.2 taels, "YT" brand was 8.075 taels, and "YP" brand was 8.15 taels. Trading was relatively active, and the market showed signs of strength.

Silk and Tea: White Silk Sales to Europe Sluggish 201

Yesterday, the local foreign firms' silk market continued to be weak. European and American markets were selling Japanese silk at low prices, while factory purchases remained sluggish. Shanghai white silk factories complained that the prices were too high and did not purchase. Yesterday, only Shen Yu and others purchased 15 bales of Shanghai white silk, and Zhonghe purchased 10 bales of white dried silk, both at flat prices.

Road Tea Firms See Brisk Sales of Fine Green Tea 202

Yesterday, the firms dealing in tea from inland routes, such as Zhen Shou, Luyongxing, Tianxiang, and Tongfu, showed strong interest in purchasing green tea bricks. Sales were similar to the previous few days. There were no large transactions in needle tea or pearl tea. No one inquired about Qining black tea. However, Tianxiang Foreign Firm purchased over 200 boxes of Yichang black tea at a price of 70 taels.

Piece Goods: Water Wave Velvet Stores See Robust Business 203

Eastern goods, having risen excessively, are not selling well. The piece goods market saw the end of the price surge yesterday, with actual sales declining sharply. This is mainly because fine broadcloth, Yuan Zhigong satin, Zhigong satin, and Yuehua velvet have all reached extremely high prices, making it difficult for customers to purchase. Furthermore, previous low-priced goods have not yet been sold off, leading to a long-term sluggishness in the market. Yesterday, only the water wave velvet stores saw brisk business. Fumeiren was sold at 0.0225 taels, Foreign Meiren at 0.023 taels, Double Dog at 0.0215 taels, Banana Leaf Title Book at 0.021 taels, and Ship Meiren Yuxian Tu were all sold out at 0.02075 taels, showing a unique prosperity. Since the price increase, many inferior brands of Yuan Zhigong satin have arrived in Shanghai, but the No. 1 brand remains out of stock. Magpie Bridge declined by 0.025 taels yesterday, and Yuehua velvet sales were very sluggish, with very few transactions in the market yesterday.

Xian Da, Wei Lun, and Sheng Da three factories jointly declare that the domestic Camel Down is first created by Xian Da, Sheng Da, and Wei Lun three factories. Therefore, the quality is excellent and the patterns are trendy, which is far better than imported goods. Although there are imitations on the market recently, the quality of the goods is rough and inferior. Compared with the products of these three factories, they are indeed very different. In order to facilitate customers to purchase high-quality domestic goods, these three factories are holding a joint promotion. Customers who want to purchase high-quality camel down can contact any of the three factories.

The mooncakes this month are not only new in style, but also specially improved in cooking. The taste is fresh, sweet, and suitable, and the raw materials are clean and beautiful. Everything is taken care of, and the material progress is shown every year. As for the sale of Guangdong mooncakes in Shanghai, the company has always enjoyed a high reputation for quality and fair price, and does not advocate hypocrisy. This year's new Liu Rong mooncakes have an excellent fragrance, and there is no match for them. There is a great demand every day. Other products such as lotus seed paste and bean paste are also selling very well, it is said.

Mingxing Film Company declares that the emotional blockbuster "Peach Blossom Lake," recently written and directed by the company's director Zheng Zhengqiu, has been working hard since the start of filming and has now been fully completed, taking more than three months. The various personnel of this film have been concentrating on the various structures of this film, which are tight and meticulous. Actors such as Hu Die, Zheng Xiaoqiu, Xia Peizhen, Wang Xianzhai, and Gong Jianong have all contributed extremely beautiful performances. This film is a domestic film with brilliant colors, which is a matter of course.

Wuchang Grand Theater declares that the theater will start showing the hilarious film "Ball King," the romantic and hilarious star Laurel Roque, who has long been famous, starring in countless blockbusters such as "The Romantic Bandit," "Ten Honest Black Gang," "Ruthless Hero," etc., all of which are popular and well-received. The new "Ball King" is his latest silent masterpiece with a complete supporting cast and hilarious performance, with bizarre interweaving and clear light. Even Roque's "Ball King" is hard to match.

Qitian Wutai declares that this stage is adjacent to the Great World on Edouard Road and specializes in performing "Journey to the West." Preparations have been underway for many years, and the construction of all parts has been completed. The construction cost is about 200,000 yuan. The first set of mechanical colored scenery is about 30,000 to 40,000. The costume item alone exceeds 10,000. Manager Sun Mutang is shrewd and capable, and Associate Ke Tianying is novel and unique in his thinking. Chen Yuelou is good at arranging new dramas. The protagonist, Little Living Monkey, has the title of Monkey King, and many famous male and female actors from Pingjin and Hankou have been hired. This stage is the incarnation of the Great World Beijing Opera Troupe, and its rehearsal skills have been honed for two years. It is indeed the originator of performing "Journey to the West." The so-called rehearsal is just the application of the latest creative and strange scenery and machinery. This stage gathers so many unparalleled talents to perform this most experienced and novel famous drama. Shanghai people will have a new experience.

Liu Wu She Box Office Since its establishment, it has been a year. Hede Road Chinese Buddhist Association declares that the association's newsletter was originally published on a regular basis, one issue per month. However, it has stopped publication since December last year, which has caused great anticipation among Buddhist monks and groups in general. In view of this, the association has decided to continue publishing, but because the delay has been eight months, it is impossible to make up for it month by month in the near future, and it is unwilling to extend it for a long time, so that there will never be a connection with the originally scheduled publication date. It has now been agreed to use an expedient method to combine the fifth and sixth issues of this newspaper into one issue, and to merge the seventh, eighth, and ninth issues into one publication. However, the content and materials will not be superficial due to the combined publication, and will still be no different from the three single-printed publications. This newspaper has already been printed and will be published soon. The combined publication of the ninth issue and subsequent issues is also being edited.

Qi Rengxi's newly compiled "Huludao" has been published by the Commercial Press. This book elaborates in detail on Huludao's terrain, historical evolution, existing facilities, and the relationship between the port opening and Northeast commerce. It also includes many exquisite illustrations such as the island's shape and work situation table. At the time of the island's construction of a commercial port, this book is really a necessary reference for us.

Inferior paper is not used. Longevity screens and orders are discussed separately. Dysentery Must Not Be Treated with Opium 224

— Feng Zhongmou

It is now late autumn, and the summer heat that was dormant in the summer has mostly broken out, whether it is autumn fever, malaria, or dysentery. Although the symptoms are different, the cause is the same. My teacher Xie Liheng (located in Ningkang Lane, North Zhejiang Road) is regarded by the medical community as an expert in treating autumn fever and latent evil, and has a unique understanding of treating dysentery. He often said that although dysentery is a serious disease, as long as the procedures are not disrupted, it is not difficult to achieve results within a time limit. The so-called procedures are: it is appropriate to unblock at the beginning, then to harmonize, then to clear, and finally to supplement. Treatment can be restored in order, but there are patients who seek quick recovery or prevent exhaustion and difficulty in support, and smoke opium to relieve temporary suffering, which often leads to prolonged and incurable cases. Therefore, this disease is mostly caused by summer dampness accumulating in the intestinal bend. The more accumulation, the more severe the pain. Only by removing the dirt and unblocking the accumulation can the disease be eliminated and the dysentery will naturally stop. If you take opium to astringe the toxic evil, it will be more imprisoned in the intestines, which is no different from recognizing thieves as sons and raising thieves behind closed doors. Doctors use medicine to expel it, and patients use smoke to keep it. Expelling and keeping each other contradict each other, then the toxic accumulation will not go away, and the intestinal wall will be more easily corrupted. Moreover, dysentery belongs to the summer heat. If the medicine is used to scour the yin early, it will be damaged, and then opium will be used to dry it, then the diet will not be compliant and it will turn into aphonia, which is also incurable. Although opium is a poisonous substance, it cannot be used to treat diseases alone. It is absolutely opposed to dysentery (there are also a few cases where opium poppy shells are used for long-term deficiency), so opium addicts are most dangerous when they suffer from dysentery. Therefore, seeing ordinary people suffering from dysentery and smoking to seek temporary peace, there is no one who does not bitterly advise against it. This is the experience of Master Xie for decades, so treating dysentery often has miraculous effects. This year, there are many cases of dysentery alone, regretting the lack of common sense in the vulgar, so I wrote this to inform the patients.

Women Trafficking Investigators Will Come from the East 225

Three people, including Dr. Johnsen of the United States, have been selected

Tokyo News The Tokyo Branch of the International League of Nations Affairs Bureau announced the dispatch of the League of Nations Women Trafficking Eastern Investigation Committee. Because the Rockefeller Foundation Social Hygiene Bureau of the United States has donated 125,000 yuan for investigation expenses, three field investigators have been selected. Dr. Johnsen (Minister of Law and Temperance of the American Social Hygiene Association, Additional Member of the League of Nations Child Protection Committee) of the United States will be the chairman of the committee, Mr. Binter of Poland, and Mrs. Chadtkette of Sweden. According to the agreement of the representatives committee of the countries concerned (meeting in Geneva in late August) on the itinerary of the investigation committee, the group is scheduled to depart from Geneva at the end of September, arrive in Singapore at the end of October, and come to China via the Malay Peninsula and Annam. They will then inspect Japan until May of next year.

Number of Japanese Tycoons Increases by Two 226

Twelve people nationwide with annual income of over one million yuan

Osaka News According to a survey by the Japanese tax authorities, due to the sluggishness of commerce and industry, the determined amount of income of various operators this year has generally decreased. However, the highest-level high-income earners have increased compared with the previous year, that is, Mr. Mitsui Hachiroemon, whose income was about 2.8 million yuan last year and who is the only high-income earner in Japan, has not changed much this year and still maintains the top position in the country at around 2.8 million yuan. Mr. Iwasaki Hisaya, who ranked second with an income of about 2 million yuan in the previous year, still ranks second with an increase in income from dividend distribution of about 2.4 million yuan. The former's income tax is 740,000 yuan and the latter's is 620,000 yuan. The third is Mr. Iwasaki Komiyata with about 1.56 million yuan. In addition, there are ten other members of the same clan, Iwasaki Yata and Okura Kihachiro, Hattori Kintaro, Mitsui Genyuemon, Mitsui Motonosuke, Mitsui Takakiyo, Mitsui Takatoshi, and Mitsui Jutaro, who have been determined to be the high-income earners in Kanto, Japan, with more than one million yuan. As for the Kansai area, only Mr. Sumitomo Kichizaemon and Mr. Inui Shimpei have received the determination of more than one million yuan. Last year, Mr. Sumitomo was above Mr. Inui, but this year, Mr. Inui is more than 230,000 yuan more. In total, there are 13 people nationwide with an annual income of more than one million yuan, which is an increase of two people this year despite the sluggish market.
